Chapter 1225: Chapter 1224: Old, Can’t Keep Up with The Times

Zhongshan County, Governor Mansion’s rooftop.

The Governor Mansion was the tallest building in Zhongshan County. Standing here, County Magistrate Zhou could see the entirety of Zhongshan County’s beautiful scenery without any obstruction.

He reached out as if trying to grasp the nearby street scene, as though he could control the entire Zhongshan County with just a stretch of his hand.

The cool night breeze brushed through, stirring his thoughts.

He recalled Man Gu’s performance during the meeting tonight and could not help but clench his fists tightly, making them creak.

"With Man Gu here, this Zhongshan County is probably not mine alone."

"Sir, Man Gu was really disrespectful to you at the meeting," Zhou Hai’s personal guard stood behind him, expressing indignation on his behalf.

County Magistrate Zhou shook his head and laughed it off, "After all, he is a disciple from the Seek Dao Sect and the current top scorer. It’s normal for him to be arrogant and not take someone like me, the county magistrate, seriously." freewёbnoνel.com

A hint of coldness flashed through County Magistrate Zhou’s eyes, "But he also needs to know that it took me a hundred years to rise to this position today, and it was certainly not by being kind-hearted!"

"Even if he is a disciple from the Seek Dao Sect, after all, this world ultimately belongs to Great Xia, and the Seek Dao Sect is just one of the five Immortal Sects."

"Once in the official circles of Wild State, you need to follow the rules of Wild State’s official circles."

He had connections all over the official circles of Wild State!

Thinking of this, County Magistrate Zhou subconsciously touched the Storage Ring on his middle finger, his trump card in navigating through Wild State’s official circles.

"Where is the Storage Ring?!"

County Magistrate Zhou suddenly widened his eyes; his Storage Ring had disappeared without a trace!

That was something he absolutely could not allow others to get their hands on!

...

After the night shift, on the way back to the Government Office, Lu Yang looked at the streets, which were slightly busier than usual in the early morning, and felt puzzled.

"Old Meng, have you noticed that there seem to be more outsiders coming to our county?"

Quyi County wasn’t a tourist attraction, and logically, there shouldn’t be so many outsiders.

"Indeed, there are quite a few more, and have you noticed? All these people are cultivators, from the Golden Core, Nascent Soul, to the Spirit Transformation realms."

Compared to the number of mortals, cultivators were extremely rare. The sudden influx of so many cultivators suggested that this matter was probably not so simple.

After returning to the Government Office, the two decided to inquire with Man Gu.

"Oh, the increase in the number of cultivators? It’s because there’s a Secret Realm about to open," explained Man Gu.

"We have a Secret Realm in our county?"

"No, not here. There’s a Secret Realm left behind by a cultivator from the beginning of the Great Xia period on a mountain not far from our county. It’s called the Four Treasures Secret Realm."

Man Gu walked to the courtyard, pointing towards a distant mountain. It was early morning, and a misty fog enveloped the mountain, adding a mysterious aura to it.

"It’s that mountain over there, called West Mountain. Deep in West Mountain, there lies a Secret Realm."

"The Four Treasures Secret Realm opens once every hundred years. The Secret Realm has three levels, corresponding to the Golden Core Stage, the Nascent Soul Stage, and the Spirit Transformation Stage. Cultivators from these three realms can all participate in the trials of the Secret Realm."

"The counties near West Mountain will see a rise in cultivator appearances, and it will be lively for a while."

"We’ve only just reached the Spirit Transformation Stage," lamented Lu Yang and his companion, wishing there was a Tribulation-Passing Level Secret Realm that they could try to venture into.

The highest was Spirit Transformation Stage, so they wouldn’t interfere.

"Little Yang is really naive; only an Immortal can create a Tribulation-Passing Level Secret Realm."

"That’s also true, this level of Secret Realm isn’t something you just stumble upon."

"Even if you do run into it, there’s no need to go, right?" Fairy Eternity said matter-of-factly, "After all, it’s built by Immortals. If you want the rewards from the Secret Realm, just find the Immortal who built it and ask directly for the rewards."

"Uh, that’s not necessary either." Lu Yang, with his thin skin, could not bring himself to do such a thing.

In the following days, more and more cultivators arrived in Quyi County. Although there were many cultivators, probably because they did not want to cause trouble before the opening of the Secret Realm, they all behaved themselves, and the public order in Quyi County remained as usual.

Lu Yang and another strolled on the streets during the day, occasionally hearing exclamations.

"Look, that’s Kong Wen from White Horse Temple, it’s said that he has mastered one of the Six Spiritual Powers of Buddhism, Telepathy, no schemes can hide from him!"

"Master Shi Chan from the Suspension Temple highly praises him."

Draped in a kasaya, Kong Wen held one hand upright at his chest, chanting the Diamond Sutra, seemingly oblivious to the exclamations around him.

"The Azure Dragon Saint Son from the Quadruple Sect is also here, his Azure Dragon Killing Skill is recognized as unparalleled in this age, even comparable to a Sword Cultivator!"

"The Quadruple Sect even purchased Dragon’s Blood for him. After bathing in the Dragon’s Blood, his Azure Dragon Killing Skill has reached an initial mastery. Magic artifacts can hardly harm him!"

The Azure Dragon Saint Son, a muscular man with dragon horns, was a Dragon-man, followed by many followers.

"The Eldest Senior Brother from the Tinghai Sect is here too. Ever since most of the high-ranking members of Tinghai Sect were captured, it has been in decline. It’s said that the remaining leaders abandoned their differences, stopped their backstabbing, and started nurturing him as a seed of revival!"

"There’s also the Holy Daughter from the Seven Star Holy Land, rumoured to possibly be the next Lan Ting..."

"A direct disciple of the Sect Leader from the Shura Sect..."

Lu Yang and his companion exchanged glances, seemingly not recognizing any of these people.

"We’re old, out of touch with the times." Lu Yang sighed, his back to his companion; despite the reactions of the people around, he didn’t recognize anyone, surely a sign these were all rising talents.

"Time flies, leaving no one behind." Meng Jingzhou also shook his head and sighed.

"Wait, these people are about our age, and some are even older, like this Azure Dragon Saint Son."

Meng Jingzhou, using his Spiritual Sense with a slight probe, could determine the bone age of these individuals, all peers.

Having heard Old Meng say this, Lu Yang remembered; they had seen the Azure Dragon Saint Son for the first time, but had met the White Tiger Saint Heir during their Foundation Establishment Stage at the borders of Great Xia.

At that time, Lu Yang had just learned Imitation Fist and had kindly shaved the White Tiger Saint Heir’s head.

"Peers are only at the Spirit Transformation Stage." Lu Yang had thought peers would at least be at the Void Refinement Stage.

At least the peers he saw were all at the Void Refinement Stage, like Man Gu, Li Haoran, Tao Yaoye, Lan Ting, Shi Chan, etc.

Even Zhao Po was at the Void Refinement Stage.

"Boss, two fried dough sticks please." Passing by a stand, they suddenly felt hungry.

"Ah, this is the downside of cultivating too quickly, no common language with peers." Both sighed one after another; perhaps this was the cost of reaching the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

Kong Wen and two constables brushed past, his pupils suddenly shrinking.

Due to his Telepathy just developing, he couldn’t yet control it well. He continuously used Telepathy to hear the thoughts of those around him.

But the minds of these two constables were terrifyingly calm, completely silent to his powers!

Who are they?!

Lu Yang, eating his fried dough stick, noticed Kong Wen using Telepathy on him and flashed a profound, inscrutable smile.

The two passed by Kong Wen, who stood frozen, the sound of one of their telepathic messages echoing in his mind.

"If I were you, I wouldn’t speak of our affair to anyone."

Chapter 1226: Chapter 1225: Government Office Inspection

"Why did you send him a message?"

"To add a sense of mystery."

...

Five days later, the Secret Realm opened, and the bustling Quyi County returned to its former tranquility.

Lu Yang and his companion couldn’t be bothered to join the crowd at the Four Treasures Secret Realm, as everything happening on West Mountain was visible from the yard. The dense fog surrounding the mountain couldn’t obscure their sight at all.

They saw Cultivators forming various camps, filled with personal grudges and factional disputes, complex indeed, as if they were about to start fighting at any disagreement.

However, the Cultivators kept their wits about them and held back, opting to wait until they were inside the Secret Realm before taking any action.

As for what happened inside the Secret Realm, Lu Yang and his companion couldn’t see, but it didn’t matter much—it was just a spectacle.

After all, West Mountain wasn’t in their jurisdiction, and thus not their problem.

Two more days passed, and the Secret Realm closed.

...

"Chase! While the snipe and the clam grapple, it’s the fisherman who benefits. After all our fighting, who would have thought Ji Zhong would be the one to snatch the fruit!"

"It’s obviously you who’re targeting me on purpose!" Ji Zhong retorted angrily, skillfully evading the attacks from behind.

He clutched a ripe Spirit Fruit, the most important treasure from the Four Treasures Secret Realm. This kind of Spirit Fruit matured only once every hundred years and could improve one’s Realm by a small degree when consumed by those below the Divinity Transformation Stage.

The Azure Dragon Saint Son and others were grinding their teeth in frustration—they had come to the Four Treasures Secret Realm precisely for this Spirit Fruit!

"Dare to compete with us, a mere Loose Cultivator!"

Before the Secret Realm opened, no one paid attention to Ji Zhong, the Loose Cultivator. However, after several Divine Transformation Stage Cultivators were successively defeated, everyone realized that Ji Zhong was the dark horse of the Secret Realm, or rather, a threat.

The collective targeting of Ji Zhong had backfired, and instead, he seized the opportunity to grab the Spirit Fruit.

Only then did someone reveal Ji Zhong’s background. Although he was a Loose Cultivator, he often had incredible luck, and his Cultivation progress was faster than the disciples of the Great Sects. He also had a few experiences in fighting above his level, but those victories were so coincidental that most had assumed they were due to luck.

Now, those who knew Ji Zhong realized he had been concealing his true ability!

"We must catch him!"

Ji Zhong quickened his pace and fled West Mountain, heading straight for Zhongshan County.

It was only when he reached the county town under the jurisdiction of Zhongshan County that he noticed the problem.

Deep in the night, the town was deserted. Running to and fro so conspicuously, those tracking him could easily spot his movements.

"It seems I can only hide in this county town. Is this Quyi County?"

Ji Zhong reached a corner and was suddenly bumped by someone who seemed to be in a hurry, apologized briefly, and quickly left.

Ji Zhong’s heart tightened, and he immediately checked the Spirit Fruit.

"The Spirit Fruit is still here; it seems I was overthinking it."

Ji Zhong found a run-down inn, where the innkeeper was drowsy and nearly jumped from the startle.

"Innkeeper, I need a room. Remember, don’t tell anyone I’m here, no matter who asks!"

Ji Zhong threw down ten silvers, took the key, and hid in an upstairs room.

The Azure Dragon Saint Son and others arrived in Quyi County, frowning tightly – after all, initiating a conflict in the county town could be problematic.

"He’s hiding? Search!"

"Don’t let the government office find out about us. Cover your faces!"

...

"We’ve been crouching here for several nights, how come there is not a soul in sight?" Two constables who were behind the times strolled on the street.

"Forget it, looks like there won’t be any ghosts tonight either, let’s continue checking the inns."

Lu Yang and his companion entered the decrepit inn. Upon seeing their uniforms, the innkeeper hurriedly greeted them with a smile, "Gentlemen, what brings you here?"

"You should’ve heard from your fellow tradesmen, we’re currently checking real-name registration at inns."

This was an order from the county office, stating that there were many unregistered inns in Zhongshan County that allowed people to stay just for money, and therefore all county towns were required to investigate.

"Show us the guest list for today and let’s see if you’ve registered guests according to regulations."

The innkeeper brought out a booklet, his back breaking out in cold sweat.

This place wasn’t an unregistered inn; they always registered guests by their real names. However, he was swayed by the sight of silver and rented out a room to a guest without registration. The guest also told him not to tell anyone he was here, which hardly sounded like good news.

Lu Yang noticed the subtle changes in the innkeeper’s expression and looked at him with an almost smile, "Innkeeper, if you confess now, we’ll just give you a verbal warning and let it go. But if we find something during our search, you’ll be shut down for rectification."

"Tell us, did you register anyone without following the rules?"

The innkeeper stammered in fright, "Th-there is one."

"Where?"

"Room one with the character for ’earth’."

Lu Yang and his companion went to room one with the character for ’earth’. There wasn’t a sliver of light in the room; it seemed unoccupied.

"Anyone there? Open up."

No response.

"Government office room inspection," Lu Yang stressed his identity.

Still no response.

Meng Jingzhou, growing impatient, pushed open the door and caught Ji Zhong, who was about to escape through the window.

"So it’s you who didn’t register with your real name?"

Ji Zhong was shocked. Not wanting to cause trouble and trying to escape, how could a constable have caught him?

He was a Divine Transformation Stage Cultivator!

Meng Jingzhou dragged Ji Zhong back to the room, where Lu Yang pulled out some papers, lit a candle, and began taking notes on the table.

"Name?"

"Ji Zhong."

"Produce your identification."

"Here."

"What’s your cultivation level?"

"Initial Stage of Spirit Transformation."

"Do you know it’s illegal to check in without real-name registration?"

"I do."

"Knowing that, you did it anyway?"

"I am carrying a valuable treasure. After I came out of the Four Treasures Secret Realm, I’ve been chased..."

...

The innkeeper heaved a sigh of relief when he saw that neither Lu Yang nor his companion had any intention of blaming him after they went upstairs.

Suddenly, a stout man led several people into the inn.

The innkeeper shuddered upon seeing the stout man—the Azure Dragon Saint Son from the Quadruple Sect, whom he had seen on the street a few days prior.

The Azure Dragon Saint slapped the table, causing the innkeeper to tremble with fear.

"Innkeeper, I need some information. Has anyone checked in recently and told you not to mention they’re here?"

The innkeeper was too scared to speak and could only nod in response.

"So they are here." The Azure Dragon Saint Son smiled. Ji Zhong’s Concealing Technique was really quite clever; even with Spiritual Sense, he couldn’t be found.

"Which room is he in?"

"Third Grade number one room."

"Is anyone else in the room?"

"There... there might be two more people inside."

The Azure Dragon Saint Son snorted coldly: "I knew there were accomplices!"

But the fact that there were accomplices didn’t matter to him; they outnumbered them.

Leading his followers, the Azure Dragon Saint Son stormed up to the second floor and kicked open the door of the Third Grade number one room.

"Ji Zhong, I advise you to hand over the goods obediently!"

Inside the room, Ji Zhong sat up straight, and two constables were busy taking notes.

This scene was entirely unexpected by the Azure Dragon Saint Son.

Especially when one constable stood up and sneered, "What’s this, a robbery right before our eyes?"

Constable Meng loosened his wrists and ankles; it had been a long while since he had encountered someone this brazen.

The Azure Dragon Saint Son, not wanting to get involved with government officials, attempted to flee, but before he could turn around, Constable Meng pinned him to the ground and tied him up.

His followers were tied up along with him.

"It seems you were telling the truth. You hid in the inn anonymously to evade pursuers, so we’ll overlook your offense," Lu Yang said.

"Continue. Who else is after you?" Lu Yang continued to take notes seriously, as Ji Zhong’s status had now changed to that of a victim.

"There’s someone from the Tinghai Sect..."

At that moment, the door was kicked open again by someone else, just as furious: "Azure Dragon, I heard you’re here, you won’t beat me to it—the Spirit Fruit is mine!"

The others chasing Ji Zhong took note of the odd situation with the Azure Dragon Saint Son; having been in the rundown inn for so long without leaving, Ji Zhong was definitely here!

"He’s the Eldest Senior Brother from the Tinghai Sect," Ji Zhong identified on the spot, and Lu Yang nodded, taking the information down.

Meng Jingzhou got up, tied up the Eldest Senior Brother from the Tinghai Sect, closed the door, and returned to his seat.

"Who else?"

"There’s the Sect Leader’s closed-door disciple from the Shura Sect..."

The door was kicked open yet again: "Ji Zhong, hand over the Spirit Fruit!"

"Is that him?"

"Yes."

In no time, the geniuses who had come for the Spirit Fruit were tied up one by one by Meng Jingzhou, filling the whole room.

Meng Jingzhou shook his head helplessly at the sight; taking notes on so many robbers would take a long time.

"Check the record to see if everything you’ve said is included and let me know if there are any mistakes."

Ji Zhong’s head was in a whirl—the swift change of events caught him off guard, and he couldn’t comprehend how all the geniuses chasing him had been captured?

These were all peerless geniuses, each displaying their Divine Abilities in the Four Treasures Secret Realm, favorites to claim the prize, yet not one could withstand a single move from the constables!

Still dizzy, he checked the notes and said in confusion: "There are no mistakes."

"Then sign at the bottom of each page, and on the last page write ’I have read the above notes and they are consistent with my statement.’ Wherever you write, press your fingerprint and also on the seal creases."

"Alright."

After signing and pressing his fingerprints, Ji Zhong took out the Spirit Fruit from his chest, only to abruptly change color.

It was a fake Spirit Fruit! Someone had switched the Spirit Fruit!

It was that person who had bumped into him!

He hesitated for a moment before saying, "Gentlemen, I’ve lost my Spirit Fruit. May I report it missing?"

Chapter 1227: Chapter 1226 Instigator

"The Spirit Fruit is gone?" Lu Yang asked.

Meng Jingzhou nodded.

Why do things keep happening one after another in the middle of the night? Not only have we captured a group of robbers, but now we’ve stumbled upon a theft case?

We came here to catch ghosts. Where are the ghosts?

Normally, after receiving a report, we should take a statement, but considering that taking a statement now could delay us and potentially allow the thief to escape, we’ll have to fill out the statement after catching the thief.

"Tell us what happened; when do you think it was stolen?"

"Someone bumped into me right before I arrived at the hotel..." Meng Jingzhou shared his suspicion.

After hearing this, Lu Yang and his companion had a general understanding of the case and got up to pack their things.

"Alright, you wait here; we’re going to catch the culprit."

Meng Jingzhou opened his mouth, looking at the room full of geniuses bound by Meng Jingzhou, terrified.

With Meng Jingzhou here, these people didn’t dare do anything, but once Lu Yang and his companion showed their capabilities, merely being tied up might not be enough to hold these geniuses.

Lu Yang noticed Meng Jingzhou’s concerns, swept his gaze over the geniuses, and commanded coldly,

"[No one move]"

The intangible rule was set, and the geniuses felt something beyond ropes binding them, rendering them unable to move even a little despite their efforts.

They panicked, this power was only ever felt when facing their sect elders.

This was the power of the [Rule]!

To establish such a rule so effortlessly that it suppressed them, this power was even more formidable than their elders’!

Who exactly are these two constables!

Isn’t it said that great powers like to disguise themselves as street beggars? Why have they now disguised as constables?

Lu Yang and his companion leaped out the window and flew over Quyi County. At the same time, they expanded their Spiritual Sense to envelop the entire city, searching for any suspicious cultivators.

The two locked onto a figure that blended perfectly into the night, strolling leisurely on the street. Numerous cultivators passed by him without noticing his presence, showcasing the extent of his stealth technique.

"Found him!"

The figure continued to leisurely walk down the street, humming a tune, tossing the Spirit Fruit around. Even when he saw two patrolling constables nearby, he ignored them.

Just as he passed by the two constables, they both struck, pinning him down and subduing him.

"You, you can see me?!"

The figure was shocked; this was impossible!

"A Nascent Soul Stage managing to steal from someone in the Divinity Transformation Stage? You’re quite skilled," Lu Yang teased.

Meng Jingzhou managed to obtain the Spirit Fruit in the Four Treasures Secret Realm, and it certainly wasn’t due solely to luck; his abilities were among the best even at the Initial Stage of Spirit Transformation.

But this little thief being at the Nascent Soul Stage and still being able to steal from Meng Jingzhou showed that his skills were formidable.

He must be kept under strict watch.

Meng Jingzhou snatched the Spirit Fruit, frightening the thief into silence.

He was proficient in Space Technique, capable of instantaneously moving to another location, but when he secretly tried to activate the Space Technique, he found that the surrounding space was completely locked; there was no escape!

It wasn’t even an intentional space lock; they were just so powerful that they unintentionally distorted the space!

Was it just bad luck stepping out today? Where did these two deities spring from?

"Instead of learning good, you only know how to steal," Meng Jingzhou said after confirming the Spirit Fruit was real, tapping the thief on the head.

"What’s your name?"

"Fang Ning, two lords above, this is really the first time I’ve made a mistake—please spare me, I dare not do it again!" As Fang Ning spoke, he burst into tears, his face streamed with mucus and tears, touching anyone who saw him.

Lu Yang and the other remained unmoved, deceiving others was one thing, but trying to deceive them with such fake crying was another.

Besides, having cultivated thievery to such a perfected extent at the Nascent Soul Stage, it was apparent that this wasn’t his first offense.

Considering his skills, it was feared that the local constables would find it hard to catch him once Fang Ning committed a crime.

"Search him."

Meng Jingzhou grabbed Fang Ning’s wrist, and Lu Yang searched him, quickly finding a storage ring that seemed very expensive just by its style.

"Is this the storage ring you stole?"

"No, this is my storage ring."

"Then open it."

Fang Ning hesitated, and from his reaction, Lu Yang concluded that indeed, it was the stolen storage ring.

Days had passed since Fang Ning stole the ring, and due to the overly complex seal attached to the ring, he couldn’t open it; he had been studying how to unlock the ring these past few days.

"The seal is quite intricate," Lu Yang remarked. With a slight movement, he sent out a Sword Qi and forcibly broke the seal of the storage ring.

Lu Yang took out the contents of the ring—just a few items, suggesting that its owner didn’t use this storage ring often.

Among the items in the ring, a book caught Lu Yang’s attention: ’Hundred Officials’ Descriptions?’

Although unsure of the content, its title alone seemed completely unrelated to Fang Ning.

"Where’s your identity proof?" Lu Yang now suspected that even the name Fang Ning was fake.

"I didn’t bring it," Fang Ning said earnestly.

"Where did you leave it, take us there."

"In Yunzhou," Fang Ning deliberately named a distant place.

Lu Yang was unfazed, "No problem, we can make a trip."

Fang Ning was on the verge of tears; this was the first time his schemes had backfired.

A calm voice came from the end of the street as a middle-aged man in a black robe and cap walked towards them.

"Hehe, the young disciple was merely completing my test, my friends. Could you consider letting him off this time for my sake?"

"Master!" Fang Ning called out excitedly, deeply moved—had his master been secretly watching over him as he completed the test?

After the middle-aged man appeared, the surrounding air seemed to solidify with his presence. He emitted an aura like a fierce beast of the Desolate Ancient, terrifying to the extreme, chilling to the bone.

"Encouraging theft and still talking sense? Arrest him!"

Lu Yang and his companion moved simultaneously, frightening the middle-aged man so much that he withdrew his aura and dodged quickly. Why were they fighting without a word?

Couldn’t they all, being in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, sit down and talk?

Just as Lu Yang and his companion were about to touch the middle-aged man, he instantly reappeared ten meters away.

"Space Technique? No, just pure high-speed movement." Lu Yang raised an eyebrow, such quick movement at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage was rare—this speed might even compare with the Black Feather Venerable of the Kunpeng Clan.

The middle-aged man was secretly shocked; usually, those who engaged him for the first time mistook his speed for a Space Technique. Who exactly were these two who saw through this at a glance?

Of course, Lu Yang and his companion could see through it; the Vaste Sea Ancestor often demonstrated the embryonic form of Spatial Dao Fruit before them, they couldn’t be more familiar with what a Space Technique looked like.

"It’s rare for someone of the Human race at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage to reach such speed, are you the Thief Ancestor?"

"No, the Thief Ancestor has only one leg which is why he claims to be unrivaled in speed, and no one disputes this."

"In that case, you must be the Thief King!"

"Ah? Master, you’re the Thief King?" Fang Jin was utterly shocked; his master had never revealed his true identity.

The middle-aged man remained silent, as if a single move from the opposition could expose all his secrets.

Chapter 1228: Chapter 127: Earthquake in the Wild State Officialdom

"Oh, this is a Space Projection," Immortal Fairy Eternity indeed knew the reason. ƒгeeweɓn૦vel.com

"Space Projection?"

"It happens when a Space Crack appears and the people in that space are standing right atop it, casting part of their projection here."

"The true bodies of these people are in another space. Of course, you can’t touch them."

"Are Space Projections rare?" Lu Yang considered how many Secret Realms he had been through and how many spaces he had seen. His Green Peak Sword even came with a small space of its own, yet he had never encountered a Space Projection before.

Immortal Fairy Eternity nodded: "Quite rare. Immortal has only seen it a few times."

Shock crossed Lu Yang’s face; indeed, the occurrence was very uncommon.

"Mainly because only unstable spaces with cracks can cause a Space Projection, and spaces become unstable when the Cultivator building them lacks the necessary skill."

"Usually, Cultivators are aware of their level, whether they are good at the Space Skill or not. Those who are skilled build spaces, those who aren’t skilled, don’t."

"It is rare to see someone who is unaware of their own level and dares to haphazardly build spaces."

"The hauntings the Barbarian lad spoke of must be the Space Projections, which have been occurring for four months now."

"After four months, the master of that space is still unaware of the Space Crack; you can imagine his skill level."

The figures still caught up in the Space Projection were talking.

"Don’t worry, the official ritual will definitely have no issues. Look, we’ve conducted a trial run of the ritual every month, four times now, isn’t every time a success?"

Lu Yang: "..."

I think your trial runs weren’t very successful.

Chapter 1232: Chapter 1231 Fengdu

Lu Yang mentioned the spatial projection to Meng Jingzhou, who suddenly realized what was happening.

"Spatial projection? This is actually the first time I’m hearing about it."

"No wonder Junior Brother Man thought it was a haunting."

Spatial projections were visible but intangible, and each time one appeared, Man Gu’s cultivation level would fluctuate to a very low state, preventing him from making an accurate judgment.

Whether it was a haunting or spatial projection didn’t matter anymore; after laying in wait for so long, they had finally found the main event.

"Fairy, is there a way to enter this space?"

Lu Yang was a cultivator who knew his own limitations, aware that he was not adept at the art of space and needed to consult an expert.

"It’s quite simple, really. This space doesn’t seem very stable. You could just strike a slash at the crack with a sword, or the Meng Family Kid could throw a punch, and that would create an opening."

"Is there another method?"

A twitch ran through the corner of Lu Yang’s eye; he merely wanted to inform the space’s owner to patch up the crack so as not to frighten people with these spatial projections.

If he were to attack with a sword and Old Meng with a punch, then tell the master of the space that there was a fissure, that would be no different than provocation.

"Self-detonation would also work, and make an even larger opening."

"Any methods that don’t create openings?"

Fairy Eternity spread her hands: "Then I can only ask you to have the Vast Sea Ancestral Master pick the lock."

Lu Yang scratched his head in some difficulty. Technically, both he and Old Meng were at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, nearly at the peak of their powers. It was somewhat embarassing that they would need to call on an Ancestor for help when facing difficulties.

After Lu Yang explained the situation, Meng Jingzhou also felt embarassed.

Just as the two were considering other approaches, they both felt a warmth in their chests. Upon checking, they saw that it was a message from Mu Baiyi, sent through the Jiuyou Order.

"This year, after years of effort, Fengdu is finally complete, towering and magnificent, interfacing with the heavens and the earth, sharing existence with the nether. This event is a once-in-a-millennium occasion, stirring attention from all corners. We hereby set the celebration for the completion of Fengdu on July 15, and on behalf of the entire Jiuyou Sect, we sincerely invite the Young Sect Master to grace the event."

"Entrance location: Great Xia Desolate State Zhongshan County’s ’Come Again BBQ Shop.’"

The two silently put away the Jiuyou Order.

It seemed they now knew who the owner of the space was, so there was no need to trouble the Vast Sea Ancestral Master for help.

"If I remember correctly, has the Jiuyou Sect always dreamed of establishing Fengdu?" Lu Yang had heard from Li Haoran about the significance of Fengdu to the Jiuyou Sect, but constructing Fengdu was too costly, and Qin Haoran had always disagreed with the initiative during his tenure.

Now that the barbecue shop and solar energy business continued to grow stronger, they finally had the funds to construct Fengdu.

Thinking about it, Lu Yang could be considered one of the founders of Fengdu.

"July 15? So that’s in seven days?"

Now that they knew the reason behind the hauntings, there was no need for them to patrol every night.

After informing Man Gu about Fengdu, Man Gu was quite surprised; he had said there was something sinister about the haunting incidents, and it turned out to be this.

"Will the two Senior Brothers be going?"

Lu Yang smiled, "This is a major event happening in our jurisdiction; naturally, we should take a look."

Seven days later, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou changed their appearances to that of the Young Sect Master Lu and the Dragon Saint and arrived at the Zhongshan County branch of the ’Come Again BBQ Shop.’

Mu Baiyi stood at the entrance of the barbecue shop, eagerly anticipating, and finally his wait was over as the two men arrived.

"Young Master Lu, Dragon Saint, it’s been a while since we’ve seen each other."

To Mu Baiyi, these two were no less than lifesavers. The barbecue shop not only helped him pay off his loans but also supported the establishment of Fengdu.

Alongside Mu Baiyi, the higher-ups of the Jiuyou Sect were there to greet the two men, showing their respect and recognition for the Heavenly Court Sect.

"I have long heard of the great names of Young Sect Master Lu and Dragon Saint," said the Grand Elder of the Yaoyang Sect, Liu Zhen, upon their first meeting. "This is my first time meeting you."

In the Extreme Northern Lands, Lu Yang and his companion had previously met Liu Zhen with their true identities, but they had not yet met him while assuming their roles within the Heavenly Court Sect.

Mu Baiyi hesitantly asked, "May I know where your Protectors are? Could they make an appearance? Ah, of course, if it’s not convenient, then never mind."

In his memory, every time he met Young Sect Master Lu and the Dragon Saint, there were always Protectors by their side. Why were they absent today? Was it because they were very confident in their surroundings at the Jiuyou Sect?

Lu Yang and his companion simply smiled, and a terrifying aura enveloped the entire barbecue restaurant.

"Does Sect Leader Mu think we still need Protectors now?"

Mu Baiyi, Chi Sect Leader, and Liu Zhen suddenly felt as though they were suffocating, staring at Lu Yang and his companion in disbelief.

They were all at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage—to be able to exert such oppressive force that made them feel suffocated was impressive.

"Pass Tribulation Peak?!"

Upon first meeting, they had discovered they could not see through the Cultivation Levels of Young Sect Master Lu and the Dragon Saint, but they hadn’t thought much of it, assuming it was due to magic artifacts that hid their true strength.

They hadn’t considered the possibility that it might be at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. After all, considering their youth, even prodigies like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou would be at the Early Tribulation Stage at most.

Had these two actually ascended to the Pass Tribulation Peak without any signs?

Was this the legacy of the Heavenly Court Sect?

No wonder Protectors were unnecessary; with such a Cultivation Level, they could roam the world with impunity.

People often debated who was stronger between Lu Yang and the Young Sect Master Lu. As the years passed, with the Young Sect Master Lu seldom active and Lu Yang creating various legends in the Cultivation World, people gradually leaned toward the view that Lu Yang was stronger than the Young Sect Master Lu.

Even people like Mu Baiyi thought so.

Today, the truth was revealed: Young Sect Master Lu’s infrequent activity was due to his intense Cultivation in seclusion.

While everyone thought Lu Yang was the pinnacle among Geniuses, it turned out Young Sect Master Lu’s talents far surpassed Lu Yang’s!

Liu Zhen felt that he had lived his years in vain.

"Please come inside," they said as the two retracted their aura, and Mu Baiyi quickly invited them into the Fengdu Space, his attitude even more enthusiastic than before.

In the courtyard of the barbecue restaurant stood a swirling Spatial Gate.

As they walked through the Spatial Gate, the scene changed from light to dark; the Fengdu Space was dimly lit, casting an oppressive atmosphere.

The Fengdu Space was vast, with various buildings forming a city greater than Zhongshan County, its scale grand enough to rival that of the Imperial City.

No wonder Junior Brother Li said that building Fengdu was expensive; just from these buildings, it was clear this was a major project.

Moreover, the architectural style didn’t resemble that of Great Xia at all, giving off an ancient and old-fashioned aura.

Ghost fires were the only source of light in Fengdu Space. Two green flames drifted beside them, casting their faces in a greenish hue, perfectly matching the style of Fengdu.

Chi Sect Leader and Liu Zhen were also experiencing the splendor of Fengdu for the first time, overwhelmed by the grandeur of the Jiuyou Sect’s undertakings.

No wonder Mu Baiyi was always so particular about money; it turned out all the funds had been funneled into this place.

"This architectural style is quite interesting, who designed it? Sect Leader Mu, was it you?" Lu Yang asked with a smile.

Mu Baiyi shook his head. "These were based on the sketches left by the former sect leader, Qin Haoran."

"Sketches?"

"His sketches depicted Fengdu, featuring a very unique architectural style. We’ve analyzed his designs, and they do not match the architectural styles of Ancient Times, nor those of Great Qian, Great Yu, or Great Xia."

"It is said that Qin Haoran was a man of Reincarnation. We believe the Fengdu he drew wasn’t the product of imagination, but rather that his memories of the Reincarnation Land had not completely faded, and he still remembered what it looked like."

"It’s this space that I constructed myself." Mu Baiyi said proudly.

In order to build the Fengdu Space, he had specifically learned the Space Skill; he had no experience prior to this, but now it seemed he had a natural talent for spatial matters, learning it with ease.

Chapter 1233: Chapter 1232: Ghost Food Source

"Is it different from the architectural style of Ancient Times?" Lu Yang asked with a laugh, seeming to have heard something very interesting.

"Could it be... it isn’t?" Mu Baiyi’s confidence wavered at the sound of Lu Yang’s laughter, considering that he was a true genius from the Ancient Times and the most authoritative on ancient architectural styles.

"Let’s walk and talk," Lu Yang said with a smile, signaling Mu Baiyi to lead the way.

"This way."

Mu Baiyi gestured invitingly, leading everyone to a riverside.

The fog thickened in the river, and a wooden boat anchored on the bank awaited them. Vice Sect Hierarch Shi Huagu untied the ropes, ready to ferry the group across.

"This place is called Wangchuan River, built according to the manuscripts left by Qin Haoran. Wangchuan River surrounds Fengdu, and to enter Fengdu, one must be transported by the Ferryman to cross the river."

"This river can detect dangerous items among the possessions of its passengers. Of course, you all need not be checked," Mu Baiyi added quickly at the end, so as not to offend Lu Yang and the others.

Ghostly green large lanterns floated in the middle of the river, the same color as the ghostly flames lighting their path above.

"It does have its charms," Meng Jingzhou remarked offhand as if he was very knowledgeable about these things.

"Young Sect Master Lu, where did Fengdu’s architectural style originate from?"

Instead of answering directly, Lu Yang posed a different question, "Sect Leader Mu, when do you believe the Ancient Times ended?"

"Clearly, with the Ancient Immortals turning stars into continents. After that, the Ancient Times ended, and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and others built the Great Qian Dynasty on the ruins."

Lu Yang shook his head. "That’s wrong. The time between turning stars into continents and the establishment of the Great Qian Dynasty spanned a hundred thousand years. During these hundred thousand years, a massive entity emerged, known as the Fire Dynasty."

"What?!"

Both Mu Baiyi and Chi Sect Leader Liu Zhen were shocked, and Shi Huagu, rowing the boat, nearly lost his oar and fell into the river upon hearing this secret history.

A massive dynasty spanning a hundred thousand years was unheard of by any of them.

"Do you remember me saying that back in the Ancient Times, the Heavenly Court and the Underworld stood together? One governed the living, and the other the Reincarnation."

"The Underworld that governed life and death was established during the era of the Fire Dynasty."

"The Fengdu that your sect built, indeed, has some resemblance to the locales of the Underworld."

Yingtian Immortal, Time Immortal, Immortal Jiuchong, Qinghe, and Ao Ling had lived through the Fire Dynasty’s era. Lu Yang had a general idea of what the Underworld looked like from their descriptions, which closely resembled Fengdu before him.

It was uncertain whether Qin Haoran had recalled memories from his first life by chance or had fully awakened them when he drafted the blueprint of Fengdu.

Lu Yang leaned toward the former; after all, if Qin Haoran had fully regained his memories and still failed to Pass Tribulation, that would be quite preposterous.

"So that’s how it is!" Mu Baiyi was convinced that inviting the Heavenly Court Sect was the right decision, as only someone from there would know such ancient secrets.

Everyone disembarked, and the magnificent and imposing ancient city of Fengdu revealed itself, solemn and majestic, exuding an indescribable sense of antiquity.

This ancient feeling manifested not only in the architectural style but also in the construction materials.

Lu Yang touched the city wall and asked, "These bricks aren’t newly made, are they?"

"Young Sect Master Lu has a keen eye; we happened upon the ancient capital city of the Great Qian Dynasty during our tomb exploration and used its bricks to construct Fengdu."

"All these bricks are?"

"All of them."

Lu Yang fell silent for a moment; Fengdu’s scale was comparable to the Great Xia Imperial City. If the bricks used for Fengdu all originated from an ancient capital city, it meant that this ancient city was as large as the Great Xia Imperial City.

Which ancient capital city of Great Qian could be this vast? It seems you might have stumbled upon Great Qian’s Imperial City itself.

The city gates, as heavy as mountains, creaked open to reveal a dense multitude of ghosts within. Their forms varied widely—some as tall as two-story buildings, others merely the size of a palm, with their numbers reaching into the tens of thousands.

During the grand opening festival of Fengdu City, the streets were adorned with lanterns and banners, and large red paper was pasted on every ghost—although Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang knew that Sect Leader Mu’s intentions were good, the scene combined with Fengdu’s dim environment and the green ghostly fires, looked incredibly eerie, no matter how one looked at it.

"Starving Ghost, Five Ghosts, Beautiful Ghost, Ears and Eyes Ghost..."

Lu Yang considered himself knowledgeable about various specters, yet there were many whose names he could not recall, and whose origins he did not recognize.

Sect Leader Mu introduced with pride, "The ghosts of Great Xia are almost all gathered here."

Originally, the Jiuyou Sect did not have this many ghosts, but with the proliferation of barbecue restaurants, employees would seek out ghosts in their spare time. If they were successful in recruiting them to the Jiuyou Sect, they would receive a considerable reward depending on the ghost’s cultivation level.

This would have been entirely unfeasible for the previously impoverished Jiuyou Sect.

"Based on the needs of the ghosts, we have also established academies, taverns, teahouses, and other places, enough for them to live here indefinitely."

Lu Yang had an epiphany, "So you’re saying that Fengdu City was specifically built for the ghosts to live in?"

No wonder the Jiuyou Sect was so intent on establishing Fengdu City; it wasn’t just a matter of faith, but also this.

"What do these ghosts eat, then?"

As they say, without Yin there is no growth; without Yang, there is no life. Although ghosts were beings of extreme Yin, they still needed a significant amount of Yang Qi to maintain basic activities. ƒreeωebnovel.ƈom

This is why ghosts would siphon off the living’s Yang Qi.

With so many ghosts living in Fengdu, the Jiuyou Sect surely couldn’t be capturing people regularly to feed them?

"That’s where we have to thank Chi Sect Leader."

Chi Sect Leader smiled slightly, raising his hand modestly, "I’ve only provided a bit of help. The main solution was your own idea."

"Please take a look at this," said Sect Leader Mu, pulling out a lamp from behind.

"A solar-powered lamp?" Meng Jingzhou was puzzled, weren’t solar-powered lamps supposed to restrain ghosts?

"This one is different from the ordinary solar-powered lamps."

Sect Leader Mu pressed the switch. The solar-powered lamp lit up faintly, not as bright as the ghostly fires above everyone’s heads.

"Ghosts feed on Yang Qi, and if we talk about the largest source of Yang Qi, it has to be the Sun."

"However, the Sun is too strong. Only the King of Ghosts can operate under the Sun. Ordinary ghosts would perish at its sight and cannot absorb the Sun’s energy."

"Therefore, the solar-powered lamp can perfectly absorb the Yang Qi of the Sun. I asked Chi Sect Leader to research a less bright solar-powered lamp. With lower brightness, the released solar energy would be less, and the ghosts could then assimilate it."

"I just wanted to try it out; I didn’t expect it to actually work," laughed Sect Leader Mu, having been unsure initially.

Having resolved the ghosts’ food source issue, the spirits of Great Xia would naturally flock to join the Jiuyou Sect.

The Yaoyang Sect was very willing to cooperate with the Jiuyou Sect, even offering to provide solar-powered lamps for free. Their creed was the promotion of the great Sun, and now even the ghosts had to rely on the Sun, which was sufficient to demonstrate the Sun’s greatness.

"Does this mean that these ghosts will all live in Fengdu from now on?" Lu Yang asked, sensing an unexpected boon.

Ghosts were universally acknowledged as difficult to manage by the dynasty, and there was endless debate over whether they even had rights, with no consensus in sight.

If all the ghosts resided in Fengdu, it would be ideal.

"Not all will live in Fengdu. We still need ghosts to run the barbecue joints and to work with the Yaoyang Sect on researching new products."

"Can’t you use living people?" asked Meng Jingzhou.

Sect Leader Mu waved his hand, "Using people would necessitate paying them a salary, which is too expensive. Using ghosts only requires providing them with Yang Qi."

Chapter 1234: Chapter 1233: The Strange Sapling

Hearing this, Lu Yang secretly transmitted a message to Meng Jingzhou, "That said, Old Meng, if you shed some blood, could you also attract a large group of ghosts to work for you?"

Moreover, the ghosts that would be attracted are King of Ghosts, the lower-level ones wouldn’t even have the life to drink Old Meng’s blood.

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes, "If only the King of Ghosts could outcompete the Vast Sea Ancestral Master."

Meng Jingzhou felt that the happiest person about his ascension to the Transcendence Tribulation Stage was his own ancestor, the second happiest was undoubtedly the Vast Sea Ancestral Master.

Mu Baiyi led everyone into the core area of Fengdu City, and Lu Yang noticed that Fengdu City had not only ghosts but also many people who seemed to be followers of the Jiuyou Sect.

That made sense, establishing Fengdu was a major event, so naturally, the Fengdu Festival was an occasion where all Jiuyou Sect members would gather.

Lu Yang guessed correctly; today was a big day for the Jiuyou Sect. All the barbecue shops had been closed for days, all rushing here in advance, with Lu Yang and his group being the last batch to enter Fengdu.

"Are these bricks also moved from the Great Qian Ancient City?" Meng Jingzhou stomped his feet a couple of times, feeling that these bricks and the city walls weren’t from the same era.

"No, only the city walls of the Great Qian Ancient City are usable. The quality of the stone bricks isn’t good enough to be used."

"Then where did these floor tiles come from?"

"I asked the people from the Heavenly Strategy Sect to calculate where there could be a large number of very old bricks. They came up with a general location, and after we dug around, we discovered an ancient capital city from the Great Yu Dynasty and moved all the bricks here."

Meng Jingzhou: "..."

Why does it sound like your Fengdu is put together with bits and pieces from everywhere?

"Speaking of which, your sect believes in reincarnation. In ancient times, the Underworld was indeed the land of reincarnation. Does Fengdu have the function of reincarnation as well?" Lu Yang asked.

Chi Sect Leader and Liu Zhen perked up their ears, they too were very interested in the reincarnation preached by the Jiuyou Sect.

They had also heard from the Jiuyou Sect that the previous sect leader Qin Haoran was a person of reincarnation. At first, they didn’t really believe it, but just now when Young Sect Master Lu mentioned that the manuscript left by Qin Haoran depicted the exact image of the Underworld from ancient years, this matter became very intriguing.

The affairs of the Fire Dynasty should be known to no one, how did Qin Haoran know about it?

Mu Baiyi shook his head gently, "Young Sect Master Lu and Dragon Saint have overestimated us. Currently, Fengdu City is only being used as a residence for ghosts. Although we have built Fengdu strictly following the manuscript left by the former Sect Leader, establishing the Three-Life Stone, Yellow Springs Road, and other places, they are merely replicas without the function of reincarnation."

"However, we believe that as long as our faith is strong enough, one day Fengdu will become the land of reincarnation!"

Lu Yang actually wanted to say don’t get your hopes up too high. Even the Underworld of the Fire Dynasty didn’t have the function of reincarnation, and in ten thousand years, only Li Hao became a person of reincarnation.

Thinking about it, he decided not to voice this thought; it’s not easy for them to build a Fengdu after all, so better not to discourage them.

Lu Yang thought the number of ghosts upon first entering the city was already plenty, but it wasn’t until they arrived at the heart of Fengdu City that they really understood what a mountain and sea of ghosts meant.

They even saw the true forms of the few figures from the space crack a few days ago; they were all ghosts.

So, it couldn’t be said that Man Gu made a wrong judgment; there really were ghost disturbances in Quyi County.

"Here is the sacrificial altar."

Many people and ghosts surrounded the altar, and upon seeing Mu Baiyi and the others coming over, they consciously made way.

The altar was circular and had four levels, corresponding to heaven, earth, humans, and ghosts. It was pure white, the only white in Fengdu, and very eye-catching.

"Please take your seats."

Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Chi Sect Leader, and Liu Zhen, being at the Transcendence Tribulation Stage, sat in the front row, with the high-level members of the Jiuyou Sect beginning from the second row.

"Sect Leader Mu, why is there a tree in the middle of the altar?" Lu Yang asked, puzzled.

In the middle of the altar was a circular hollow, growing a sapling over two people tall, with branches holding something unknown, tightly wrapped by leaves.

Lu Yang had seen many spirit trees in the Medicine Garden, but none that matched this sapling.

"Old Meng, do you recognize this tree?"

Meng Jingzhou was also wondering what the Jiuyou Sect was up to, "I don’t recognize it."

"Fairy, do you recognize it?"

Fairy Eternity frowned slightly, "Strange, Immortal has not seen such a thing before."

Mu Baiyi explained, "Actually, we don’t know what it is either."

"It didn’t exist when the altar was first established. Suddenly one day, a subordinate came to report that the altar had been shattered by a sapling."

"At that time, I was very surprised. The altar was made of flawless jade, which is extremely hard. We had a tough time just processing the jade stones. How could a sapling shatter it?"

"When I went to see for myself, it was indeed the case. The altar was cracked into pieces, and a never-before-seen sapling was growing."

"I asked around, but no one knew the origin of the sapling."

"Considering the sapling was quite peculiar, I didn’t dare to pull it out. Instead, I had to find another place to build the altar. But then the sapling moved locations and shattered the new altar again."

"By the third time I was rebuilding the altar, I watched the sapling day and night. I noticed that the sapling would gradually become illusory, and then a phantom of it would appear inside the altar nearby."

"When the sapling on my side completely vanished, a real sapling would appear inside the altar and then explode, shattering the altar."

"Having no alternative, I had to order a hole to be dug in the center of the altar to allow the sapling to grow. Now, it’s grown this tall."

After listening, Lu Yang was still thoroughly confused. What in the world was this sapling?

"Are those hanging from the branches fruits?"

Mu Baiyi still shook his head, "I don’t know."

The appearance of the sapling didn’t interfere with the completion of the Fengdu Festival celebration. The believers simply took the sapling planted here as having some kind of symbolism.

As the ceremony’s host, Mu Baiyi put on a black ceremonial robe and ascended the altar.

Seeing Mu Baiyi take the stage, the members of the Jiuyou Sect all fell silent simultaneously, looking up at Mu Baiyi with devout and clear eyes.

Mu Baiyi’s expression solemn, he took out the willow branch that was inserted in the jade vase and placed it in the four cardinal directions - east, west, south, and north.

The willow branch symbolized rebirth, and the four directions represented the world. The essence of reincarnation is rebirth, and the act symbolized Fengdu as the reincarnation land for the entire world, the starting point of new life.

Then, with one hand holding the ritual sword and the other the jade ring, he struck them together, producing a clear sound, all the while reciting ancient blessing words in the Ancient Language.

Lu Yang, even when translating it into modern language, still couldn’t understand what Sect Leader Mu was saying.

As Sect Leader Mu reached the midpoint of his recitation, those below started to chant along, accompanied by ancient ceremonial music.

"Lucky day, propitious hour, joyfully celebrate Jiuyou..."

The entire Fengdu City was enveloped in a solemn and majestic atmosphere, as if in resonance with heaven and earth, the space itself trembling.

Lu Yang was gradually moved by this atmosphere, and settled down to experience the process.

At the top of the sapling, the leaves unfurled and revealed a glimpse of the true nature of what was enveloped inside.

It was a fruit so illusory that it was nearly transparent, fantastic and bizarre, as if it should not exist in this world.

Witnessing this scene, Lu Yang’s pupils contracted sharply. The altar was in the center of Fengdu City, the focal point of all the believers’ attachments; in other words, it was where the Power of Faith was most abundant. The fact that the sapling only grew on the altar implied that its existence was inextricably linked to the Power of Faith!

Now, as the festival officially began, the fruit on the sapling grew at a speed visible to the naked eye.

Could it be that this thing is...

Just as Lu Yang reached this point, an untimely laughter echoed overhead, interrupting the festival proceedings, and with the laughter, the ghostly flames in the sky above Fengdu City one-by-one extinguished.

"Jiuyou Sect, you do have some skill. You’ve actually managed to create the outline of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit!"

Chapter 1235: Chapter 1234: Robbing in front of our Heavenly Court Sect?

"Indeed, it’s the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype!" The sudden figure confirmed Lu Yang’s guess.

The situation of the Jiuyou Sect was somewhat similar to that of the Eternity Sect; both used the Power of Faith to condense a Dao Fruit Prototype.

The difference was that the Eternity Sect worshipped an "Immortal Eternity" that didn’t exist, so they not only used the Power of Faith to condense the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit but also created a Fourth Housekeeper.

Whereas the Jiuyou Sect simply believed in reincarnation, so they only condensed the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype.

"Who are you, daring to intrude upon our sect!" Mu Baiyi roared with rage. The Fengdu Festival was held in the highest regard by the Jiuyou Sect, seen as the pinnacle of the Power of Faith with the emergence of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype as the best example.

The Jiuyou Sect wouldn’t allow anyone to disturb this celebration.

That figure took out a blood-stained long stick, pointing it at Mu Baiyi, the stick’s body pitch black, dyed by the blood of slain enemies, turning from red to black over the years.

"I am Si Heng God Monarch, here under the orders of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord to pluck the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype. If you know what’s good for you, retreat immediately. If not, you can’t blame me for being unfeeling!"

"Si Heng God Monarch?" Lu Yang narrowed his eyes. According to confessions from prisoners of the Great Qian Dynasty, Si Heng God Monarch was a capable lieutenant of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, in possession of a Yin Yang Dao Fruit Prototype, not condensed from the Power of Faith but comprehended through his own enlightenment.

No wonder his timing was impeccable, showing up just as the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype appeared. The Great Qian Dynasty was best at using the Power of Faith to condense a Dao Fruit Prototype.

Si Heng God Monarch had likely been waiting for the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype in the Fengdu Space.

The appearance of Si Heng God Monarch shocked all Jiuyou Sect believers, but they were not frightened, rather enraged, throwing things like teacups, plates, and solar lamps at the airborne Si Heng God Monarch.

With a cold snort, Si Heng God Monarch opened a barrier that prevented these objects from hitting him.

"Fools, it seems the world has forgotten my legend after I haven’t acted for three hundred thousand years!"

"Then try me!" Standing his ground in Fengdu, Mu Baiyi showed no signs of fear.

Moreover, since he had already stated that the fruit on this sapling was the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, he couldn’t afford to back down.

Si Heng God Monarch swung his bloody long stick at Mu Baiyi.

"Abyss Hell’s Big Grinding Plate!"

The Big Grinding Plate appeared, laying before Mu Baiyi.

"You think something like this could stop me!"

A boom resounded—before the Big Grinding Plate could show its mystery, it was smashed to pieces by Si Heng God Monarch.

However, behind the Big Grinding Plate was not Mu Baiyi, but six pitch-black coffins.

"Rise!"

Mu Baiyi shouted, and the lids of the coffins flew open as six corpses stiffly bounced out of them.

"These six are what Junior Brother Li spoke of as the Jiuyou Sect’s strongest foundation, right?" Lu Yang asked Meng Jingzhou through a psychic message.

"Pretty much."

In times of life and death, the Sect Masters of the Jiuyou Sect would control these corpses for battle.
