This wasn’t fire, but rather his qi and blood power was so abundant that his pure yang aura burnt the surrounding spiritual energy.

Anyone who got close would find their own pure yang aura ignited, which was why the Thief King dared not approach Meng Jingzhou.

The burning of pure yang aura had never happened from ancient times till now. If one had to give it a name, it could be called the Pure Yang Domain.

As for the shadow Meng Jingzhou, what he exhibited was naturally the Pure Yin Domain.

Meng Jingzhou’s fist technique was supremely yang and incredibly domineering, while shadow Meng Jingzhou’s fist technique was supremely yin and ultimately soft, as good as water. With yin and yang clashing, it was like the sun and moon competing in splendor, resembling Tai Chi, making the onlookers marvel.

The six shadow figures sustained heavy injuries from the Thief King’s attacks, and the six former Jiuyou Sect Masters soon claimed victory. Mu Baiyi intended to control these corpses to help Meng Jingzhou.

However, with the extremely intense pure yang and pure yin energies on Meng Jingzhou’s side, the corpses couldn’t get close, so they could only watch from a distance.

Fighting against his complete opposite, Meng Jingzhou grew more and more agitated. Even Old Lu had started to engage with a Semi-Immortal, yet here he was, trapped by the little tricks spun by the Si Heng God Monarch.

Whatever move he made, his opponent would counter with the exact opposite.

"I just don’t believe it!"

Meng Jingzhou, determined, stripped off his upper clothing ready for a big battle.

Then he saw his opposition also beginning to undress.

"Don’t copy that!"

Meng Jingzhou, in desperation, unleashed the Supreme Pure Yang Dharma Image and smashed it towards his opponent, blocking his further actions.

While everyone watched Meng Jingzhou’s fierce battle, a figure appeared at the edge of the altar, stepping onto it and poised to dig out the sapling and the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype.

"Who’s there!" Mu Baiyi was the first to notice the commotion, bellowed out, and the six corpses of the Tribulation Crossing Sect Masters made their move, bombarding the figure with six ultimate techniques.

After they acted, Mu Baiyi regretted it, as the figure was too close to the sapling and could harm it.

But to Mu Baiyi’s astonishment, once the smoke cleared, the figure and the sapling were completely unharmed.

How did he do it?

"As a subordinate of the Emperor, you may also call me Lord Si Shi," said the shadowy figure.

Man Gu was startled; Lord Si Shi was the last of the Great Qian’s Four God Monarchs. Could it be that Great Qian had sent two Divine Monarchs to the Fengdu Space?

It was said that Lord Si Shi’s survival of the fittest Dao Fruit Prototype was condensed through the power of faith. In terms of talent, he was not as good as Si Heng, but due to the special nature of his Dao Fruit Prototype, nobody wished to clash with him.

Upon suffering the same attack twice, it would become very difficult to harm him.

To fight with him, one must employ a different tactic each time.

"Well, I’ll be taking this Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype. No need to see me out; I know the way."

Lord Si Shi smiled, revealing eight snow-white teeth, and picked up the sapling and ran.

By the time Mu Baiyi reached the altar, the other party was nowhere to be seen.

Humming a tune, Lord Si Shi left the Fengdu Space and arrived in Zhongshan County.

He came to a tea house in Zhongshan County, which at this time was empty except for one tea customer who had not been moved from the uppermost floor.

The tea patron was watching the confrontation between Lu Yang and Si Heng God Monarch, not expecting Si Heng God Monarch to fare so poorly, being suppressed by someone from later generations.

"This youngster named Lu Yang truly possesses some extraordinary abilities."

Lord Si Shi bowed his head with clasped hands, "Reporting to Emperor Lord, the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype has been retrieved."

"Oh?"

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord ceased to watch the battle, the outcome of the fight between Lu Yang and Si Heng God Monarch was of no consequence, retrieving the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype was the mission that had now been accomplished.

"So this is the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, that after swallowing and refining one could live another life even after perishing?" A rare smile appeared on the face of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord.

As the founder of the Great Qian Dynasty who ruled over the world, Mid-heaven Emperor Lord wielded countless rare treasures, but none as precious as the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype.

He had arrived in Zhongshan County very early, waiting for the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype to mature. He hadn’t come in person to retrieve it, because he held a psychological shadow from the Extreme Northern Lands, worrying that Yun Zhi might suddenly appear; hence he dispatched Si Heng God Monarch and Lord Si Shi in succession.

With the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype in hand and Yun Zhi still nowhere to be seen, it seemed he had been overly concerned.

"Emperor Lord, is this Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype really as miraculous as it sounds? How come I’ve never heard of such a thing before?" Lord Si Shi curiously inquired.

"Could it be false? This is... not something you should know."

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord couldn’t wait to grab the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, but saw Lord Si Shi retracting it.

The face of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord turned ugly in an instant, "Si Shi, what do you mean by this!"

Lord Si Shi simply smiled, as a strange voice emerged from his body.

"No meaning at all, just that the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype is known by only a few in the Fire Dynasty, and I want to know where you learned about the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype!"

Boom—

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord furiously slammed the tea table, demanding from Lord Si Shi as the teahouse collapsed with a crash, "Who are you!"

A figure exuding a ferocious aura floated out of Lord Si Shi’s bracelet, its head topped with two coral horns, its cheeks and the backs of hands covered with red scales, its pupils dragon-like, tiger-like, as if it were the supreme Venerate among demons.

"I am the Qilin Immortal that you have been searching for."

"Qilin Immortal, you’ve been hiding in Si Shi’s bracelet all along!"

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord was enraged, Lord Si Shi’s bracelet looked ordinary, he claimed it was a relic from his mother that he had worn all along, but to think that the Qilin Immortal was concealed within!

"This cannot be, if you’ve been in the bracelet all this time, why did the Seeking Immortal Token not react!"

The Seeking Immortal Token was a proud creation of Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, it would heat up whenever the Four Ancient Immortals were nearby, the closer they were, the hotter it would become.

Qilin Immortal laughed casually, "I’m afraid the Emperor Lord has forgotten my Dao Fruit is about survival of the fittest, a move only works once against me. I let Si Shi use the Seeking Immortal Token to get close to me once, after that, it became useless against me."

"Teacher." With the guidance of Qilin Immortal, Lord Si Shi could condense his own Dao Fruit Prototype, but that would make him stand out among the God Monarchs, so he chose to use the Power of Faith to condense his Dao Fruit Prototype.

Qilin Immortal took the sapling and Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, reverted his head to its original form, opened his mouth, and swallowed them, temporarily storing them in his stomach, "Si Shi, step back for now."

Si Shi tactfully stepped back, the tension between them palpable, far from a situation that looked as though it could be resolved peacefully.

"I’ll ask you one more time, who told you about the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype!"

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord glared daggers at the Qilin Immortal, his teeth clenched in anger. He had tried every means to find the Four Ancient Immortals, not expecting that they were right beside him, playing him for a fool, "If I told you, would you give me the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype?"

"No."

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord immediately expanded a vortex that devoured everything, "Then there’s no more need for words, let’s see who’s truly stronger!"

Chapter 1240: Chapter 1239: All Too Familiar

The Thief King finally ended his inner struggle and decided to go against his conscience to help Lu Yang.

"I’ll help you..."

Before the Thief King could finish, he heard a thunderous boom behind him. A monstrous tidal wave of energy erupted, flinging him into the air, making it impossible for him to stand steady.

Turning his head, the Thief King saw two figures emanating terrifying auras in a standoff, surrounded by ruins under their feet.

And that wasn’t all. As the auras from the two figures grew even more terrifying and rapidly spread outward from them as the center, wherever his gaze fell, Zhongshan County turned to ruins.

Frozen in place and allowing the cold wind to howl through him, the Thief King’s heart sank in despair.

What use is it that I’ve outlined the Speed Dao Fruit?

"Mid-heaven Emperor Lord?"

"Qilin Immortal?"

Lu Yang and Si Heng God Monarch were startled to see the two combatants and, in a tacit understanding, ceased their fighting, with the Yin Yang Body of Si Heng God Monarch merging into one.

Lu Yang was utterly confused seeing the Immortals battle. It made some sense for the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord to appear here since it could be explained that he, being cautious by nature, sent Si Heng God Monarch to test the waters while he waited for good news outside.

But the question was how the Qilin Immortal had suddenly appeared, and why were the two of them fighting each other?

Fairy Eternity was lying on a bed within the Spiritual Space, legs kicking up and down in the air, instructing Lu Yang on how he should fight Si Heng God Monarch: "Little Yang, you should fight like this... Huh, why is the Qilin Immortal here?"

Seeing the Qilin Immortal in battle, Fairy Eternity suddenly perked up, climbed up from the bed, and watched the Immortal Battle intently.

"That’s not the right way to fight. Why defend now? Go for a mutual injury strike. Little Yang, go over there and tell him how to fight!"

Lu Yang looked towards the center of the battlefield, felt a sense of futility, and quietly withdrew his gaze.

Fairy, leave me a way out, will you?

"Are you Lu Yang?" Lord Si Shi flew over—or rather, was blown over by the blast of the battle.

"My name is Survival God Monarch Si Shi. If it’s a hassle, feel free to call me Lord Si Shi," Lord Si Shi introduced himself in a rather familiar manner.

Having captured so many Great Qian prisoners, Lu Yang of course recognized Lord Si Shi.

"What are you here for!" Lu Yang watched Lord Si Shi guardedly. The God Lords of Great Qian were supposed to be his enemies, yet something about this didn’t feel right.

"My teacher said if he got into a fight with the Emperor, I should stand by your side. If you’re lucky, you might survive."

"Who’s your teacher?" Lu Yang, utterly confused, thought it might also be due to Fairy Eternity constantly prattling in the Spiritual Space, affecting his thinking.

"Si Shi, why are you standing with the enemy!" Si Heng God Monarch shouted angrily.

Lord Si Shi spread his hands: "Isn’t it obvious? I’ve defected."

"You!"

Si Heng God Monarch was so choked up he couldn’t speak.

"I advise you to stand over here too, it’s safe." Lord Si Shi kindly offered advice to his former colleague, noting that observing the Immortal Battle up close was extremely dangerous.

Si Heng God Monarch, though not book smart, was no fool. He sneered, seeing through Lord Si Shi’s intention: "You think I would believe a traitor’s words? I’ve already seen through your schemes. You must want to lure me over there and then join forces with Lu Yang to capture me, making me a Confession!"

Just then, without any sign, Lu Yang shuffled a few steps to the side, and Lord Si Shi quickly followed.

Si Heng God Monarch did not understand the move, but suddenly from the center of the Double Immortal Battlefield, an attack flew over, directly hitting where Lu Yang was just standing. It struck Si Heng God Monarch, who instantly exploded with injuries all over his body.

"Cough cough cough—" Si Heng God Monarch’s body rapidly healed.

Every living creature is composed of Yin and Yang, and as long as one maintains the balance between the two within the body, one can prevent all illnesses and heal wounds spontaneously.

Suddenly another aftershock flew over, and Si Heng God Monarch couldn’t dodge in time. He was blasted beyond recognition. On the other hand, Lu Yang seemed to foresee the future, predict where the aftershock would appear, and avoided it in advance.

Si Heng God Monarch chose to trust the traitor’s words and approached Lu Yang cautiously, step by careful step, and only when he saw that neither Lu Yang nor Lord Si Shi intended to strike him did he relax a bit.

It was Fairy Eternity who had anticipated the incoming attack and advised Lu Yang to move aside earlier.

"How come you all are together?" The Thief King regained his senses and, finding Lu Yang and the two Great Qian God Lords standing together, chatting and laughing, felt like he had missed something and curiously flew over.

"Young Sect Master," Lu Yang greeted respectfully.

The Thief King waved his hands frantically, "No, no, don’t call me ’senior.’ You are the senior."

The strikes that Lu Yang had directed at Si Heng God Monarch a moment ago had nearly caused him to faint from fright; he had been praying the whole time for Si Heng God Monarch to hold on.

Thankfully, Si Heng God Monarch lived up to expectations.

But considering the current situation, it didn’t seem to count for much.

As they were talking, a black vortex flew by from the Emperor Lord, passing close but not harming anyone. Nonetheless, it still made the four of them shudder.

Where the black vortex landed, only a large pit remained – the buildings and land had completely vanished.

Devouring Dao Fruit, devouring all things.

"Teacher was right; staying close to Fellow Daoist Lu Yang really does save lives," Lord Si Shi remarked with a smile. If it had been just him, he would have been severely injured long ago.

"You’re Lu Yang?" the Thief King asked in surprise.

"Yeah, what about it?" Lu Yang wiped his face, reverting it to its original look. Since entering Fengdu Space, he had been using the appearance of Young Master Lu, and even before that, when he was a constable, he had used another face. It was normal for the Thief King not to recognize him.

The Thief King’s expression turned increasingly strange: "My master is the Thief Ancestor."

The Thief King had become a disciple after being captured by the Thief Ancestor, and it was from the Thief Ancestor that he learned the key to condensing the Speed Dao Fruit Outline. However, the Thief Ancestor had stopped teaching him during the final step, leaving him to comprehend it on his own.

"Your master is the Thief Ancestor?" Lu Yang heard the insinuation in the Thief King’s words; the Thief Ancestor and Daoist Buyu were sworn friends, which made them peers.

The Thief King nodded, pretending to chat while probing for information: "By the way, I heard from Lord Man that Zhongshan County bought insurance. Do you know about this?"

"Yeah, I suggested Junior Brother Man buy it."

The Thief King recalled all the large transactions that had been signed at the commerce association, and to his knowledge, Zhongshan County had never bought insurance before: "When did you buy the insurance?"

"Seven days ago."

The Thief King: "..."

So, they had captured me and immediately insured Zhongshan County afterward!?

If Lu Yang didn’t know the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and Qilin Immortal, he would have suspected that Lu Yang had colluded with these two Immortals.

Wait, didn’t one of the Great Qian God Lords just refer to Lu Yang as "Daoist"? What’s Lu Yang’s relationship with the Great Qian Force?

"Who’s the teacher you’ve been referring to?" Lu Yang turned to ask Lord Si Shi.

"The Qilin Immortal. He said you know him."

Lu Yang nodded; of course, he knew the Qilin Immortal. Although they had never met face to face, he was quite familiar with him: "What else did Qilin Immortal Senior say?"

"He said you should be quite familiar with the Immortal Fairies."

Lu Yang’s face turned ashen.

Listening from the side, the Thief King felt more and more that there was something extraordinary about Lu Yang.

Chapter 1241: Chapter 1240: Mid-heaven Emperor Lord Battles Qilin Immortal

Above Zhongshan County, there was a battle of blood between two Immortals, shattering the void and turning all in their path to nothingness. fгeewёbnoѵel.cσm

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord stood in the midst of a pitch-black vortex, the space near the vortex distorted, and time slowed to a crawl.

Suddenly, a black vortex emerged behind the Qilin Immortal, and one of his arms was viciously torn and devoured, blood streaming down.

The Qilin Immortal’s face was dark and grim as he concentrated his will on the severed limb, which regrew as if by self-healing.

"Hahahahaha, after all those grand claims, Qilin Immortal, is that all the power you possess!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord laughed wildly. His Devouring Dao Fruit could swallow anything; even an Immortal Body was consumed entirely by him. If this happened a few more times, even if the Qilin Immortal could regenerate a severed limb, he wouldn’t last long.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord was not worried about accidentally harming the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype in the belly of the Qilin Immortal. Rather, it would be just right to devour and refine it.

"This much power is enough to deal with you," came the response.

As his words ended, the Qilin Immortal let out a long howl, as if tilting heaven and earth, in the star-studded Ancient Times. Yet, this roar alone could cause the galaxy to dissolve into countless meteors streaking across the universe.

The Buddhist Lion Roar was like an ant shaking a tree in the face of the true Qilin Roar.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord stamped his foot fiercely, creating ripples in space that collided with the Qilin Roar. The sky shook, the earth sank, and Lu Yang and three others not far away joined hands to withstand the impact of the shockwave.

"Quick, cover your ears!" the Thief King used his Spiritual Sense to urgently remind everyone as he saw the scene unfold.

"Don’t cover your ears; it won’t block it, counter with a soundwave attack!" Lu Yang also used his Spiritual Sense to shout.

All four were somewhat proficient in soundwave attacks, and even though their skills varied, they all knew moves like the Buddhist Lion Roar.

Si Heng God Monarch, Lord Si Shi, the Thief King, three of them mimicked the howls of Demon Beasts, while Lu Yang’s voice stuck out among the four, using the Fairy Shout.

However, his was also the most effective, blocking the majority of the soundwaves that reached them with the Fairy Shout.

It was just that the others gave Lu Yang strange looks.

The winds changed, thunder sliced across the sky, and Zhongshan County was covered by dark clouds, with countless tornadoes spiraling into being, wrapping wind, rain, thunder, and lightning within.

As the only Kirin among heaven and earth, the Qilin Immortal was a favorite of nature, inherently intertwined with natural phenomena. Although his mastery over thunder and lightning wasn’t on par with the Yingtian Immortal, aside from the Yingtian Immortal, no other Immortal’s lightning spells could surpass his.

"As the Emperor who shares a lifespan with heaven and earth, how could thunder and lightning harm me!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord stood immovable in the face of the apocalyptic onslaught of thunder and lightning.

The sky reverberated with the deafening boom of thunder, aiming straight for the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, but the pitch-black vortex devoured the thunder, leaving him unscathed.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord snapped his fingers, and the dark vortexes spread across the entire space. The newly regrown arm of the Qilin Immortal, along with a leg, was once again swallowed. That was the source of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s confidence—his Devouring Dao Fruit was both offensive and defensive, capable of guarding against Immortal Techniques and devouring Immortal Bodies, leaving his foes powerless.

The Qilin Immortal’s body grew back once more. This was not some magic skill, but a natural self-healing ability he was born with.

"I’d like to see how many times you can heal!"

The dark vortex once again swept in, completely engulfing the Qilin Immortal, distorting space, nullifying any Space Spells there, and twisting time to make the Qilin Immortal’s movements extremely slow.

The previous two times, the Qilin Immortal somehow managed to dodge the vortexes, but this time, he made no move to escape and merely stood there.

"Have you resigned to your fate?" The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord activated his Devouring Dao Fruit, and several vortexes suddenly expanded to fully envelop the Qilin Immortal, the ease of it making the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord wonder if the one standing there was just a Puppet of the Qilin Immortal.

"Emperor, is that all the power you have?"

The Qilin Immortal stood amidst the black vortex, completely unharmed!

"If it were the Yingtian Immortal, dealing with you would indeed be restricting. Unfortunately for you, you’re facing me," the Qilin Immortal commented with a smile.

"The Dao Fruit of the Fittest! You intentionally took the hits the first two times to adapt to my attacks!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord instantly realized that the same attacks could no longer injure the Qilin Immortal.

Facing the assault of the Dao Fruit Prototype, the Lord Si Shi could only avoid most of the damage, and couldn’t remain untouched. The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord hadn’t expected that the Qilin Immortal, as a bearer of an Upper Dao Fruit, could so remarkably adapt even to attacks from the Dao Fruit itself.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s face gradually became overcast with shadows, "It seems that to defeat you, I must use different techniques."

"Three Flavored True Fire!"

"Qingtian Prison Suppressing Hand!"

The Hand of Heaven descended from above, ablaze with the mighty Three Flavored True Fire, and the palm was filled with Magic Runes that bore the power to suppress and destroy. A single rune could obliterate all of Zhongshan County. The vast number of runes were clenched within the Hand of Heaven, and their collective force was unimaginable.

The Qingtian Prison Suppressing Hand was a technique the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord had chanced upon in ancient tomes, one that he had never used before, and even The Controller didn’t know he could perform it.

This technique was tremendously powerful and was not inferior to the Buddha Land in Palm.

With a thunderous crash, the Hand of Heaven suppressed the Qilin Immortal, who simply raised a hand without a hint of Mana fluctuation, and caught the formidable punch.

"Three Flavored True Fire and Qingtian Prison Suppressing Hand, huh? You’ve mastered them well. Unfortunately, these techniques are useless against me, as I have already seen them in Ancient Times," the Qilin Immortal retorted nonchalantly.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s face turned ashen. A great many of his techniques originated from Ancient Times, and without anyone to teach him, he had managed to master the essence on his own—a rare talent in the world.

But this also meant that the more he had mastered the essence, the more useless his techniques became against the Qilin Immortal. Most of his repertoire had no effect on his opponent.

"As your senior, I’ve already allowed you three moves. If you have no other techniques, it’s my turn now," the Qilin Immortal confidently declared.

With a shake of his form, the Qilin Immortal transformed into a golden Qilin, stepping on auspicious clouds, rising through the mists, a sight of majestic awe. In Ancient Times, even placing his image on a door could ward off evil and protect the household.

"Do you think I only know ancient techniques?"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, always appearing with the air of a senior in the present era, was inwardly prideful. Now the Qilin Immortal was claiming to be his senior, boldly asserting to have given him three moves, which immediately incensed him.

"Taiyi Seven Killings Palm!"

"Liangyi Micro Dust Formation!"

"Creation Heaven Technique!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord unleashed three successive Immortal Techniques, each a self-created move powerful enough to establish a sect and serve as the trump cards for those at the Pass Tribulation Peak and at the level of a Semi-Immortal.

The Liangyi Micro Dust Formation trapped the Qilin Immortal, with the Taiyi Seven Killings Palm claiming life with each strike. The seven palms layered over one another were so potent that not even Heaven could save the victim, and the Creation Heaven Technique could prevent the Qilin Immortal from healing his wounds.

"How have I never seen these techniques even once?" Si Heng God Monarch exclaimed in surprise.

As the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s confidant, even if the Emperor Lord had kept some techniques from him, it shouldn’t have been so many.

Trapped in the Liangyi Micro Dust Formation, the Qilin Immortal defended while taunting, "Ha, sealed by Wu Yao in the Sun for one hundred thousand years, you really have come up with quite a few tricks."

"Shut up!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord grew furious. The life span of Semi-Immortals was limited, and in order to wait for the Great Era, they had been slumbering throughout the entire Great Yu Dynasty. The fact that Wu Yao had sealed him in the Sun was only known to The Controller.

Little did he expect that the Qilin Immortal had been hiding in Lord Si Shi’s body and witnessed the whole process.

Chapter 1242: Chapter 1241: The Strength of Qilin Immortal

The Taiyi Seven Killings Palm not only contained a killing intent in each palm strike, but the seventh strike could stack the killing intents of the previous six strikes, an assault even Immortals couldn’t withstand.

He had now executed six palm strikes, each accurately hitting the Qilin Immortal. After receiving the six strikes and having his healing abilities suppressed by the Creation Heaven Technique, the Qilin Immortal’s blood wouldn’t stop flowing.

"Taiyi Seven Killings Palm, the seventh strike!"

The seven killing seals overlapped, and dark strength erupted within the Qilin Immortal’s body, but the expected bleeding from seven orifices did not occur. The Qilin Immortal remained unharmed except for spitting two mouthfuls of black blood, which compared to the first six strikes, was not a severe injury.

What was happening, had the seventh strike been adapted by the Survival Of The Fittest Dao Fruit?

This shouldn’t be, the move was called the Taiyi Seven Killings Palm, but it was actually a combination of seven techniques. Logically, the Qilin Immortal shouldn’t have adapted to this move, and if he had, he wouldn’t be spitting blood.

Why exactly?

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord realized the Qilin Immortal was absolutely no ordinary foe, donned his Immortal Gold Armor, and went to battle a second time.

Though it seemed the Qilin Immortal was at a disadvantage, continuously taking hits, he felt an unsettling sensation within, as if he were overlooking something.

The Qilin Immortal had adapted to the Liangyi Micro Dust Formation and could no longer be restrained by it. With a long cry, he charged once more at the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, emanating the supreme pressure of the Supreme Demon, actually completely overshadowing the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord in terms of aura.

But how could the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord be suppressed by mere aura? He struck with formidable power, carrying a tyrannical air exclusive to the supreme of this world.

"Kill!"

The sky stirred violently, like thunderclaps roaring. The Immortal Gold Armor, moving with his will, split and transformed into a great spear, clashing with the blood of the Qilin Immortal.

Just as the Qilin Immortal was about to make contact with the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, he suffered an invisible attack and staggered, breaking his momentum.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord seemed to have anticipated this, sweeping his spear across and colliding with the Qilin Immortal’s antler. The spear, unable to withstand the antler, shattered upon contact but immediately reformed.

"Is this the method of The Controller?" Lu Yang frowned. The scene he had just witnessed was too reminiscent of The Controller—using spiritual essence for attacking the Qilin Immortal, the Immortal Gold Armor’s transformation at will, and its autonomous defense capabilities.

He recalled the three Divine Monarchs he encountered at the Laurel Fairy Palace, who mentioned that the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord could consume other Dao Fruits but needed the Laurel Tree Ancestor to enhance his spiritual power.

"Does that mean he’s consumed the Enlightenment Dao Fruit Prototype, or a part of its powers?"

The Qilin Immortal, naturally hiding within the body of Lord Si Shi, could come to the same conclusion.

However, the time was ripe, and it no longer mattered.

"Soul Chasing and Soul Capturing!"

Seeing that he couldn’t overcome the Qilin Immortal by force, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord unleashed a mental attack, striking directly at the primordial spirit and soul, undeniably unblockable.

But the Qilin Immortal merely shook his head and continued to look vibrant.

"This is impossible!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord had tried this move on The Controller before. Only with precaution could The Controller barely withstand it; the Qilin Immortal couldn’t be unharmed.

The Qilin Immortal had adapted to the Creation Immortal Technique, and his injuries began to heal on their own. His blood roared vigorously in his veins, resonating with heaven and earth, a sight truly horrifying.

He galloped on all fours, each movement seeming to manipulate the world. The spiritual attacks commanded by the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord could not halt the Qilin Immortal’s steps or momentum. The wisps of aura he emitted crushed the earth and shattered mountains, revealing ravines.

The Immortal Gold Armor sensed danger, transformed into a shield, and positioned itself entirely in front of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord.

But it was all futile; the Immortal Gold Shield only slightly slowed the Qilin Immortal’s pace before shattering upon impact. The antler struck horizontally, blasting two large holes in the chest of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s eyes widened in disbelief. When he first battled with the Qilin Immortal, the latter was never this powerful.

Had he been hiding his true strength previously?

No, he was getting stronger in battle!

"Fool, fighting a protracted battle with the Qilin Immortal, the longer you fight, the stronger he gets!" Fairy Eternity laughed heartily in the Spiritual Space, never having expected that the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord would engage the Qilin Immortal for so long.

"Little Yang, did you figure out the reason?"

"The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord was deceived by the name of the Dao Fruit," Lu Yang roughly guessed the reason.

"The Survival Of The Fittest Dao Fruit is not only the Upper Dao Fruit for the ’Survival Of The Fittest Dao Fruit Prototype’ but also for the ’Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit Prototype’ and ’Natural Selection Dao Fruit Prototype.’"

"In other words, he has the abilities of these three Dao Fruit Prototypes and they have been enhanced."

The reason Ao Ling was known as the top among Semi-Immortals, is because she possessed the Natural Selection Dao Fruit Prototype, growing stronger the more she was attacked.

"That’s also why the Qilin Immortal predecessor’s early stage was about defense, rarely attacking; he grew stronger in this manner."

Originally, battles among Immortals emphasized the use of Dao Fruits. However, if the gap between the two parties was too great, and considering most of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s moves were ineffective against the current Qilin Immortal, the outcome of this battle was predictable.

The Qilin Immortal reverted to human form and grabbed the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord by the neck: "I’ll ask you once again, who told you about the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype!"

Recognizing the gap between himself and the Qilin Immortal, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, devoid of the will to resist, truthfully replied, "It was the one who had fought with you, the Four Ancient Immortals. He told me that refining the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype could allow one to live another lifetime even if the Immortal perished."

Seeing this, Lord Si Heng panicked; the Emperor was captured, and three Semi-Immortals stood beside him, one renowned for his speed, making escape impossible.

What did I say, this is a trap!

Thief King, facing a legend like the Qilin Immortal, the foremost among the Supreme Demons, and a revered figure by the Demon Race, was instinctively nervous.

I have been proud of this for three hundred thousand years.

Chapter 1245: Chapter 1244: Unexpected Change

Then why don’t you hold onto it, Fairy?

Even as a captive, he wouldn’t normally reveal everything so readily!

The Qilin Immortal scoffed, "Forgotten, have you? My Dao Fruit is the Upper Dao Fruit of the ’Survival Of The Fittest Dao Fruit Prototype’!"

The Survival Of The Fittest Dao Fruit Prototype grants the victor dominion over the vanquished—Zhu Tian relied on this power to firmly secure the throne of Demon Emperor.

As both the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and the Qilin Immortal were Immortals, naturally the former wouldn’t be entirely dominated. However, it was effortlessly simple for the Qilin Immortal to compel the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord to speak truthfully.

Does he too wish to live another life?

With the power of the mastermind behind the scenes, he wasn’t afraid of Qilin Immortal getting the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype at all!

The figure’s laughter accompanied the ever-shifting black mist.

"What naturally born monster, nothing but a beast with no father or mother!"

Chapter 1246: Chapter 1245: The Strength of the Puppet Master

"Die for this young master!" freewebnovel.com

In the Fengdu Space, the Great Sun Crossing the Sky, Meng Jingzhou had a breakthrough in the midst of the battle, with his fist technique undergoing a transformation, truly reviving the ancient unstoppable might. What had happened? The outside world was supposed to be a fight between Old Lu and Si Heng God Monarch, wasn’t it?

Soon after, they heard the sounds of intense fighting coming from the sky. Qilin Immortal seemed to be incredibly angry, looking as though he could devour someone. Lord Si Shi had never seen his master with such an expression since he started his apprenticeship.

The three of them didn’t dare think too much and ran for their lives all over the world. They certainly didn’t dare to run towards Lu Yang; that would be even more dangerous.

...

At this time, Lu Yang was running around Zhongshan County with the Green Peak Sword on his back, having placed the seedlings and the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype inside the Green Blade Sword Small World.

Had it not been for his possession of the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit, he would have been severely wounded by the shockwaves by now.

Although Qilin Immortal was surprisingly angry, almost seeing red, the anger obviously did not enhance his combat power. He was being completely suppressed by the hidden hand behind the scenes.

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord was nowhere to be found; it was unclear whether he took the chance to escape or hide somewhere.

The true target of the mastermind behind the scenes was the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, so wherever Lu Yang fled, the battlefield would shift there, making it so that Lu Yang dared not escape into the Fengdu Space nor leave the confines of Zhongshan County. If the battlefield were to move elsewhere, it would bring catastrophe upon that place.

Lu Yang wasn’t idle either, persistently using "predict the future." Impossible futures unfolded before him, through which he confirmed that the mastermind had not used the Dao Fruit of time manipulation.

Thinking this, Lu Yang turned his head to look at the Qilin Immortal who, despite being riddled with wounds, was still roaring and howling furiously. The speed of his injuries far exceeded his self-healing rate, allowing the mastermind to suppress the Qilin Immortal with pure strength alone, without the need for Dao Fruits.

"Qilin Immortal Senior, he is trying to enrage you, don’t fall for it!" Using Spiritual Sense to communicate, Lu Yang noticed that as soon as the mastermind appeared, the Qilin Immortal couldn’t suppress his fury. After being provoked, his rage intensified—the strength of his Qi and Blood boiled over, flooding Zhongshan County, fighting recklessly as if he was courting death.

This also fit Lu Yang’s impression of the mastermind: although powerful, he preferred to use strategies. Except for the time when the Fairy Eternity met her demise and the mastermind had no time to escape and was forced into a battle with the Four Ancient Immortals, the other times the mastermind made his move, it was never done in person.

Strange, why would he take matters into his own hands this time?

Upon hearing this, the Qilin Immortal calmed down and regulated his breathing. That’s right, he was already at a disadvantage against his opponent. If he allowed himself to be led around by the nose, it would only get worse.

"Shattering Mountains and Rivers!"

The Qilin forced back the pain and stomped down powerfully, collapsing the mountains and rivers. Though calmer now, every strike he delivered was still filled with lethal intent, showing no mercy.

Even if it meant dying and his Dao dissipating today, he would take a chunk of flesh from his opponent!

"Heh," the mastermind let out an almost imperceptible laugh. With his Cultivation Level, he naturally could hear Lu Yang’s spiritual communication. But what could a mere Qilin do even if it calmed down? It would still be the loser.

Boom—

The mastermind raised his hand to block the Qilin Immortal’s hoof, yanked it downwards fiercely, and the Qilin Immortal lost control and crashed onto the earth, creating a deep pit of unknown depth.

The adversary didn’t even use any magic skills or Divine Abilities, relying only on bare-handed combat to suppress the Qilin Immortal, not giving any chance for the Survival Dao Fruit to come into play.

The Qilin Immortal opened his Storage Ring; various rare and precious immortal medicines were stuffed into his mouth like money was no object, and his injuries quickly recovered.

His horn glowed, with runes flickering. This was his innate Divine Ability: even at the Golden Core Stage, he could use his horn to shatter mountains. When contending with the Yingtian Immortal, even the Yingtian Immortal had to avoid its sharp edge.

He broke through the earth and charged at the mastermind behind the scenes. In a flash of lightning, the mastermind grasped the horn, reversed his grip, and slammed it to the ground, causing the Qilin Immortal to vomit blood heavily, with a muted sound from his body indicating numerous broken bones.

Suddenly, the wind and clouds underwent a drastic change, and the Exorcism Divine Thunder came crashing down fiercely, slamming hard into the mastermind.

An Immortal controlling the Heavenly Tribulation descended upon the world, eyes like torches, radiating a divine and majestic aura.

The Yingtian Immortal incarnation surveyed the area: the Qilin Immortal covered in wounds, Lu Yang desperately running, and that memorable silhouette shrouded in black mist. In an instant, he understood what had happened.

Couldn’t you find another way to call me here? Must you curse me!

This thought passed fleetingly, and then Yingtian Immortal’s attention immediately turned to the figure within the black mist. As always, it was difficult to deal with; even his Exorcism Divine Thunder couldn’t tear through the opponent’s black fog.

Damn, just with an incarnation, he couldn’t handle the mastermind behind the scenes.

"Ying Tian!" Upon seeing his old friend, the Qilin Immortal, lying in the pit, shouted excitedly. Among the Four Immortals, he had the best relationship with Yingtian Immortal.

"Quit the nonsense, let’s catch up later. Can you get up?"

"Yes!" The Qilin Immortal revitalized his spirit and reignited his momentum, flying up to the sky, ready to battle alongside Yingtian Immortal.

Chapter 1247: Chapter 1246: I Can Spare You

Lu Yang cursed at the Yingtian Immortal and quickly fled from beneath the Sixth Immortal, while in his Spiritual Space, the anxious urging voice of Fairy Eternity resounded.

"Is Miss Yun done?"

"Please be patient a little longer, esteemed Fairy. If we act rashly, the enemy might flee upon realizing the adverse situation. I will be ready soon."

...

Divine Thunder was clear and bright, and Zhongshan County had become an ocean of thunderbolts, with scorched earth, rolling thunder resounding through ten thousand miles of sky, and storms wreaking havoc, sending sand and stones flying. If one extended their Immortal Sense, it would be scattered in an instant, disrupting the Sixth Immortal’s perception.

Nectar descended, healing the injuries of the Qilin Immortal.

Yingtian Immortal stood amidst the ocean of thunderbolts, with three thousand Immortal Thunders above his head, and feet upon earth, fire, wind, and water; he was the undisputed master of the Heavenly Tribulation.

"Upper Pure Immortal Thunder!"

If the deployment of the Exorcism Divine Thunder when descending was an opportunistic move, then this Upper Pure Immortal Thunder was a buildup of power, incomparable in might to anything before!

The vast Immortal Thunder surged like a torrential flood, rushing toward the Sixth Immortal.

The black mist surrounding the Sixth Immortal seemed capable of blocking everything in the world, flowing upstream, targeting not the Yingtian Immortal but the Qilin Immortal.

His actions were urgent, fast, and precise; neither the Yingtian Immortal nor the Qilin Immortal could react in time.

With a thunderous palm, the Sixth Immortal pierced through the Qilin Immortal’s chest. From his chest, thunder burst forth, exploding with a bang, and the entire Immortal Body transformed into a thunderbolt.

The thunder scattered and reconvened into the likeness of the Qilin Immortal in the distance.

Having transformed into a body of lightning, the Qilin Immortal could freely traverse the ocean of thunderbolts.

Adaptation to the environment, survival of the fittest.

"A body of lightning?" The reason the Sixth Immortal did not confront the Yingtian Immortal first was that the Yingtian Immortal had descended in a body of lightning, which was difficult to deal with. He had not expected the Qilin Immortal to react so quickly and also adapt to the environment by transforming into a body of lightning.

But it was only a slight inconvenience.

"Taiqing Immortal Thunder!"

"Yuqing Immortal Thunder!"

Yingtian Immortal frantically spurred on the Tribulation Dao Fruit, forcing himself to create the Three Pure Immortal Thunders in the shortest time possible.

The Three Pure Immortal Thunders, used for slaying immortals and vanquishing demons, suppressed the world with such mighty power that once released, even the Yingtian Immortal himself could hardly control them. In Ancient Times, only Immortal Fairy had the skill to withstand this attack.

The Upper Pure Immortal Thunder transformed into a flood of thunderbolts, the Taiqing Immortal Thunder into an arsenal of ax, halberd, sword, and spear amidst thousands of Immortal Soldiers, and the Yuqing Immortal Thunder into a six-sided shield, forming a cube that sealed the Sixth Immortal, along with the Upper Pure and Taiqing Immortal Thunders, within.

The cube was dazzlingly bright, emitting full immortal light. Lu Yang merely looked up and blood streamed from his eyes, blinding him instantly. His eyes were ruined. Knowing that he was now equivalent to a Semi-Immortal, yet unable to even glance at it, one could hardly imagine the power of the Three Pure Immortal Thunders directly facing the Sixth Immortal.

Lu Yang healed his eyes using the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit and distanced himself from the battlefield as much as possible.

He knew relying solely on the Three Pure Immortal Thunders would not be enough to defeat the Sixth Immortal. If this move had been effective, the Four Immortals and the hidden hand behind the scenes would have settled their score in Ancient Times.

Sure enough, with a loud bang, the Sixth Immortal performed some technique or perhaps simply relied on sheer power to blast open a gap in the cube formed by the Yuqing Immortal Thunder. The black mist twisted irregularly, a situation not seen before, clearly indicating that the Three Pure Immortal Thunders had affected him.

In the instant the Sixth Immortal blasted the gap, the Qilin Immortal accelerated with the power of lightning. Even the Speed Dao Fruit could hardly match such velocity. His entire body transformed into a being of lightning, except for the kirin horn, which remained as it was.

The kirin horn struck the black mist of the Sixth Immortal, sinking in like a stone into the sea, and making no progress whatsoever.

Yingtian Immortal wielded an ax and hacked at the back of the Sixth Immortal’s head!

This was an Immortal Artifact hastily crafted from the materials in the Qilin Immortal’s Storage Ring, its creation rushed by necessity, allowing for only one use.

One use was enough!

The Sixth Immortal caught the ax with his hand and crushed it with force!

"It did seem a bit more coordinated than in the Ancient Times."

Before the battle with the mastermind behind the scenes in the Ancient Times, the Four Immortals mainly sparred with each other and did not have the experience of fighting together. After establishing the Fire Dynasty, they worked hard to study their own characteristics and think about how to cooperate in battle to unleash the maximum combat power.

The Sixth Immortal exhaled several kinds of Immortal Fire, which exploded upon touching the thunder bodies of the other two Immortals, shattering their bodies to pieces.

The combination of thunder and fire is the most explosive in the world; naturally, it leads to a blast when they come into contact.

As the two attempted to reconstitute their thunder bodies, the Immortal Fire continued to hunt them down, exploding once more.

Though this level of explosion could not harm their essence, it did keep them occupied with reconstituting their thunder bodies, preventing them from accomplishing anything.

"If you’re willing to hand over the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype and swear no longer to be my enemy, I can spare your lives," the Sixth Immortal said slowly, with a tone suggesting negotiation. "After all, I am not a bloodthirsty person. As long as you don’t stand in my way, what does your fate matter to me?"

The two burned with rage—The Sixth Immortal clearly did not regard them at all.

Even though they were obscured by the black fog, it was still apparent that the Sixth Immortal was shaking his head, seemingly unable to understand their actions: "Moreover, why should you sacrifice your lives for someone else?"

If the Four Immortals did not understand his strength and fought him during the Ancient Times, that would be somewhat understandable. However, having acknowledged the gap in strength after the ancient battle, they still dared to challenge him recklessly.

The Qilin Immortal roared in anger and abandoned the thunder body, reverting to his original form. These flames of Immortal Fire were of average power and only posed a threat to the thunder bodies; his Immortal Body could easily resist the flames.

The Yingtian Immortal used several pieces of Immortal Gold from the Qilin Immortal’s Storage Ring to temporarily craft some armor plating to shield against the Immortal Fire.

Neither of them answered the Sixth Immortal’s question. Their philosophies were entirely different from his. Even if they replied, what would it do? Could they possibly make the Sixth Immortal agree with their viewpoint?

"It is you who are seeking death."

The Sixth Immortal said in an indifferent tone, deciding their fate. He moved instantaneously in front of the Qilin Immortal, whose pupils contracted dramatically—The Sixth Immortal was even faster than before!

The Sixth Immortal grasped the Qilin Immortal’s neck and struck his face, causing the Qilin Immortal’s head to explode like a watermelon!

As the Qilin Immortal’s head slowly regrew, the Yingtian Immortal stimulated the Tribulation Dao Fruit to summon Nectar from heaven, which the Sixth Immortal used to smash the auspicious clouds formed from the Nectar.

Seeing the Sixth Immortal rushing towards him, the Yingtian Immortal hastily used the Thirty-three Layers Of Heavenly Tribulation to intercept, while the Sixth Immortal used the Qilin Immortal as a shield to block all Heavenly Tribulation, with his other hand seizing the neck of the Yingtian Immortal.

"You think I can’t touch you with your lightning body?"

Though within the lightning body, the Yingtian Immortal was choked with the suffocating sensation of a drowning mortal.

What kind of tactic was this?!

Suddenly, ice and snow spread for millions of miles, instantly covering the entirety of Zhongshan County in an instant. The extreme cold seemed as though it could freeze time itself, causing ice to form on Lu Yang’s body, requiring all his strength to break free!

Upon seeing this, the Yingtian Immortal immediately activated the Tribulation Dao Fruit, summoning Heavenly Tribulation once more. Rolling thunder, intermingled with endless Immortal Fire, combined harmoniously this time instead of exploding. The Heavenly Thunder induced flames from the earth like a primal cataclysm, with unparalleled might, even more terrifying than the Three Pure Ones Heavenly Tribulation. The black fog began to dissipate strand by strand, forcing the Sixth Immortal to temporarily release the Qilin Immortal and the Yingtian Immortal.

Accompanied by Immortal Fire and Profound Ice, the Immortal Jiuchong arrived, glaring at the Sixth Immortal with gritted teeth.

He had been discussing Dao with Mister Tiankui at the Five Elements Sect when he sensed a disturbance from the west, indicative of an Immortal Battle, so intense that it could be felt from such a distance.

Following the disturbance, he hurried towards the Wild State. Halfway through, the vibrations disappeared, suggesting the Immortal Battle had concluded. Out of curiosity, he continued towards the Wild State.

Approaching the Wild State, he encountered a much more intense wave of fluctuations, the intensity of the ongoing battle far surpassing that of the initial Immortal Battle!

Arriving at Zhongshan County, he saw the Sixth Immortal simultaneously restraining the Qilin Immortal and the Yingtian Immortal. Without time for further thought, he intervened, unleashing the Extreme Cold Domain to slow the flow of time and summoning Immortal Fire to attack the Sixth Immortal.

But Immortal Fire alone was not a threat to the Sixth Immortal.

The Yingtian Immortal immediately understood the Immortal Jiuchong’s intention and combined forces with Heavenly Thunder, leading to the current situation.

"Sixth Immortal..."

The Immortal Jiuchong’s roar filled with rage had not yet been fully voiced when he saw the Sixth Immortal perform a hand gesture, and ninety-nine mountains rose from the earth, flying towards the Jiuchong, hammering him into the side of a mountain. Mountain after mountain collapsed until the last one halted the impact.

Chapter 1248: Chapter 1247: Since You’re Here, Don’t Even Think About Leaving

Immortal Jiuchong tried to escape from the grip of the Sixth Immortal, but he had already witnessed the latter’s power in Ancient Times and knew that he could not compete.

In just an instant, his body exploded countless times under the attack of the Sixth Immortal.

"Switch!"

Immortal Jiuchong switched personalities, allowing his more aggressive personality to take control.

This aggressive personality didn’t mess around. Since he couldn’t confront the Sixth Immortal head-on, he changed tactics, immediately using the Earth Escape technique to burrow into the ground, escaping to the surface to regroup with Yingtian Immortal and Qilin Immortal.

"How is it outside, is the battle over?" Meng Jingzhou was restless in the Fengdu Space. He had glimpsed a moment earlier when Qilin Immortal was being suppressed in combat, overwhelmed by an unexpectedly powerful opponent.

...

The chaos, Yin and Yang, and Five Elements all intertwined, each alone was powerful enough to make any cultivator pale with fear. Heavenly Tribulations always followed the rule of "forty-nine with a slim chance of survival", but this time there was no chance at all, an unprecedented terrifying calamity since ancient times!

The Infinite Heavenly Tribulation spread far and wide, fiercely enough to scare any cultivator into losing the ability to think.

The Sixth Immortal shattered the ground with a stomp, the earth fissured, and the intensified Immortal Mountain turned into a solid Protective Shield, but it could not withstand the Infinite Heavenly Tribulation for even three breaths and crumbled.

Combining two types of Dao Fruit into one was not an easy feat without long-term integration.

"You’ve indeed worked hard to defeat me."

The Sixth Immortal maintained a calm tone, not sounding like the focus of an assault, but rather like a judge sitting high above.

At that moment, Yingtian Immortal took control of the battlefield. He used the world as a furnace, spiritual essence as kindling, and Infinite Heavenly Tribulation as fierce flames, aiming to refine the Sixth Immortal!

"So you are treating me as an Immortal Artifact to be refined. Not a bad technique."

Around the Sixth Immortal, the fog grew darker and murkier, and the Infinite Heavenly Tribulation did indeed affect his carefully refined black fog.

The Heavenly Tribulation seemed endless, and so did the black fog, leaving the fierce battlefield in a weird balance.

Suddenly, the roar from the King of Demons broke the balance, Qilin Immortal using the Infinite Heavenly Tribulation to conceal himself, waiting for the moment the Sixth Immortal became distracted to launch a surprise attack!

However, the Sixth Immortal still managed to divide his focus to deal with Qilin Immortal. He threw a punch toward Qilin Immortal, who seemed to pass through him like a phantom, his attack missing.

"A phantom? No, it’s Right-Erect Shadowless."

The Great Divine Skill Right-Erect Shadowless could temporarily turn one intangible. During intangibility, the enemy couldn’t hit you, and you couldn’t hit the enemy either.

Qilin Immortal moved behind the Sixth Immortal, exposing an open gate!

Now!

With his enhanced strength, Qilin Immortal gathered all his might, smashing his hooves fiercely onto the back of the Sixth Immortal!

The black fog on the back immediately thinned out!

Not enough!

Qilin Immortal opened his mouth, spitting out several Immortal Artifacts that Immortal Jiuchong had brought.

No matter what the original purpose of these Immortal Artifacts was, at this moment they had only one use—self-detonation!

This was the first time the Qilin Immortal had spoken since the appearance of Immortal Jiuchong.
