Through the spreading ripples, the barrier finally became visible!

Judging by the curvature of the barrier, the entire Zhongshan County was enclosed!

Someone had placed a seal while he was fighting!

He had been completely unaware of it beforehand!

"Who is it!"

He dropped Yingtian Immortal and Immortal Jiuchong, as these two were no longer important at this moment.

"Since you’re here, don’t think about leaving."

The spatial fluctuations rippled, and Yun Zhi emerged, her face expressionless.

Without exuding any aura, just standing there, she became the focus of the battlefield, providing unparalleled hope.

In fact, as early as during the battle between the Qilin Immortal and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, Lu Yang, seeing that the situation was dire and uncertain of the outcome, and with Dou Dou Fairy unable to act, had immediately called for Eldest Senior Sister.

But after the Qilin Immortal defeated the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, there had been no need for Yun Zhi to show herself; she stood by, quietly listening to the Qilin Immortal recount the course of events.

Then, when a villain from behind the scenes appeared, attempting to rob the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype, Yun Zhi took action.

In the battle at the East Sea, Yun Zhi fought Ashy Bean, who, unable to defeat her, used various escape techniques to flee.

Yun Zhi knew that the Sixth Immortal was an even more formidable presence than Ashy Bean. If he was determined to flee, even having both her and the Fairy here might not be enough to stop him.

For this reason, she had utilized the Power of National Fate of Great Xia Country to construct a barrier system within Zhongshan County to ensure that the Sixth Immortal could not escape.

Yingtian Immortal nearly laughed out loud, knowing that since Lu Yang was here, Yun Zhi would definitely appear.

They had finally made it to this moment!

Chapter 1249: Chapter 1248 Let me see who you really are!

Above Zhongshan County, the atmosphere was grim, and time seemed to freeze at that moment. No one made a move.

Lu Yang breathed a sigh of relief, he had managed to set up the barrier before the Sixth Immortal noticed.

Unnoticed, Mid-heaven Emperor Lord appeared beside Lu Yang.

While setting up the barrier, Yun Zhi had also captured the fleeing Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and entrusted Lu Yang with the important task of watching over him.

Although Lu Yang felt that Eldest Senior Sister was overestimating him,

"Emperor Lord, I advise you not to think about running away," Lu Yang slowly said, noticing that the Emperor Lord was contemplating escaping amidst the chaos.

"You once tried to secretly devour the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype. The Sixth Immortal was nearby and heard everything. Do you think the Sixth Immortal would let you go?"

The face of Mid-heaven Emperor Lord changed again and again, forced to admit that what Lu Yang said was true. The power of the Sixth Immortal was beyond his imagination.

If he were to break the barrier, not only would he be escaping, but so would the Sixth Immortal.

By the time the Sixth Immortal came looking for him, it would be a dead end for him!

The Sixth Immortal looked at the opponent, and for the first time, a hint of seriousness appeared in his calm tone. The black mist contracted to its limit, forming something resembling armor, to prevent a sudden attack from the opponent.

Then, the Sixth Immortal chuckled, "Yun Zhi, with your current state, how many more times can you act?"

"If I am not mistaken, over time, you would gradually merge with the Dao. The more you act, the faster this process will occur. What then? Do you actually wish to speed up the merging process?"

The Yingtian Three Immortals were shocked upon hearing this. What did the Sixth Immortal mean by ’merging with the Dao’?

Lu Yang, who had been ready to relax, grew serious again. The Yingtian Three Immortals might not know the details, but he understood. Could it be that Eldest Senior Sister was becoming increasingly close to the state of merging with the Dao, and unlike the first time, she might not be able to exit from this state again?!

However, the Sixth Immortal’s words did not elicit any emotion from Yun Zhi. She calmly spoke in an undeniable tone, stating two facts.

"You are wrong about two things."

"Firstly, I still have many opportunities to act."

"Secondly, you are not my opponent."

The tone of Yun Zhi changed dramatically, filled with intense anger, which was vastly different from her usual demeanor.

"Your opponent is me!"

Everyone present recognized the origin of this voice and realized what had happened.

"Has Immortal Fairy borrowed Daoist Yun Zhi’s body?!" Yingtian Immortal was astonished. Could that even happen?

Since the Sixth Immortal and Fairy Eternity were sworn enemies, naturally, Yun Zhi wouldn’t overstep her bounds and participate in this Immortal Battle.

Fairy Eternity moved her body slightly; Miss Yun’s body was indeed quite useful, allowing her to utilize her full strength.

Boom—

Fairy Eternity didn’t give the Sixth Immortal any chance to react. Her eyes cold as knives, she transformed into blazing lightning racing across the sky, fiercely punching toward the Sixth Immortal!

The Sixth Immortal, fearing no one, chose to confront the attack head-on!

As the fists collided, the black mist clinging to the fist could not withstand the force of Fairy Eternity’s punch and immediately dispersed!

"This was something only the Yingtian Three Immortals could accomplish together!"

The black mist rapidly recondensed, and the Sixth Immortal’s eyes were equally icy, "It seems your new body is indeed very useful."

Fairy Eternity had borrowed Yun Zhi’s body, making it difficult for him to bypass her and seize the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype without facing severe consequences.

It was better to look for another opportunity.

As the Sixth Immortal clashed with Fairy Eternity, her Immortal Fist Technique was overwhelmingly tyrannical. The Sixth Immortal kept retreating, moving back toward the edge of the barrier.

He seized the moment to punch the barrier, but contrary to his expectations, it did not shatter. Instead, it rippled, the waves spreading throughout and the force of his punch absorbed.

If he had time, such a mere barrier could naturally not stop him, but how could Fairy Eternity give him the chance?

"Think not of escaping!" Fairy Eternity charged forth, her presence immaculate and divine, like a Flying Immortal from Outer Space.

The two collided repeatedly, shattering the void, the aftershocks resonating, Dao Sounds echoing through the skies, and primitive runes interwove into a sea, dispersing into particles of light.

Even the Yingtian Three Immortals had never seen Fairy Eternity this furious, she was unstoppable, every entity in her path doomed. They wanted to intervene but could not act, as in such an intense battle, the rapid movements meant their attacks might hit Fairy Eternity instead of the Sixth Immortal.

The fury that Fairy Eternity felt toward the Sixth Immortal was not solely due to him killing her, but also because her death had plunged the Four Immortals into profound sadness, causing Little Lotus, Little Ling Lianyi, and the three others to remain heartbroken despite their amnesia!

And the arrival of the pitiable yet detestable Ashy Bean, the downfall of the Fire Dynasty, the Four Immortals hiding for three hundred thousand years.

Everything stemmed from her, she felt she had failed these people!

Her Immortal Fist Technique was powerful and majestic, supremely dominant, making any strong being pale in comparison.

Although it was the combined efforts of the Five Ancient Immortals that delayed the path to the Dao Fruit, in truth, Fairy Eternity alone was sufficient. In other words, in the Ancient Era, Semi-Immortals were as common as rain, all originating from Fairy Eternity!

Fairy Eternity’s fist technique was versatile and unpredictable, seemingly without pattern, yet all within the variations of her Immortal Fist Technique.

The Qilin Immortal, upon seeing Fairy Eternity executing her technique, felt a faint pain throughout his body, reminiscing about ancient times.

The Immortal Fist Technique was derived from herbs, each punch representing the effect of a different herb. Theoretically, one could adapt to the Immortal Fist Technique if struck enough times, but the issue was the new effects when different herbs were combined. The combinations were infinite and thus impossible to adapt to!

Despite the black mist continually condensing, the black mist on the Sixth Immortal’s body trembled irregularly, meaning he was struggling to control it precisely!

Fairy Eternity held back her frustration, the Sixth Immortal didn’t use the Dao Fruit, so she wouldn’t either; she wanted to defeat him fair and square!

Realizing his face was targeted, the Sixth Immortal shifted from attack to defense.

Although he momentarily held her back, he found her punches getting faster and heavier.

As the battle began, it was not Fairy Eternity’s true strength, for the cultivation systems differed and it was her first time using Yun Zhi’s body, necessitating a period of adjustment. Right now, she was gradually adapting to Yun Zhi’s body through battle.

Fairy Eternity’s eyes blazed, her fists glowing, and with a final thunderous boom, she broke through the Sixth Immortal’s arms and his facade!

Even if the Sixth Immortal tried to gather other parts of the black mist to his face, it was futile, the built-up strike unstoppable.

"Hiding in shadows, afraid to show your face, let me see who you really are!"

Boom— frёeωebɳovel.com

The black mist enveloping the Sixth Immortal was completely shattered, revealing a face all too familiar to both Fairy Eternity and the Yingtian Three Immortals!

"Yao Saint!"

The only one from ancient times who mastered the Great Divine Skill of Verbal Spell, Yao Saint.

Chapter 1250: Chapter 1249: Yao Saint

"Yao Saint, it’s you!"

Everyone was astonished; the Sixth Immortal turned out to be someone they believed had long since died, yet everyone had heard his name.

Speak and Follow Yao Saint.

"Who is Yao Saint?" Mid-heaven Emperor Lord frowned, for he had not heard the name before.

Lu Yang glanced at Mid-heaven Emperor Lord beside him, wondering how he could be unfamiliar with everyone. However, since Seek Dao Sect had a tradition of treating captives favorably, he kindly introduced, "He’s the cultivator from Ancient Times who mastered the divine ability ’Speak and Follow.’"

"Is that him?"

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord suddenly realized, aware that in Ancient Times there existed a genius who mastered the almost lost ’Speak and Follow,’ undefeated in his class and never once defeated in battle. However, he fell shortly after advancing to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, causing the divine ability ’Speak and Follow’ to become lost to the ages.

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord had sought out traces of the ’Speak and Follow’ numerous times without success.

In the era where geniuses were innumerable and Tribulation Crossing Half Immortals could be found everywhere, Yao Saint didn’t stand out much, and even his name did not survive through time.

The reason lay in the fact he had perished too soon; before the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, he indeed enjoyed unmatched glory, with his legend spreading throughout an entire star system.

But which genius from Ancient Times did not have similar legends? Which was not one to have defeated countless rivals, claimed to be unbeatable in their own class, ascending to the pinnacle of a star system atop their heads?

What truly determined their strength, however, was the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

Regrettably, Yao Saint fell too soon and did not have the chance to confront the other geniuses in battle. He died at the hands of Fairy Eternity, without even a single notable victory to his name.

Even immortals such as Yingtian Immortal had only heard the name of Yao Saint and had not crossed paths with him in combat. They had not expected Yao Saint to be such a formidable adversary.

Lu Yang remembered that, according to Fairy Eternity, she had injured Yao Saint, who had always protected himself too well and rarely took a hit. He cried out "It hurts to death," and consequently, he died.

His death was somewhat abrupt; talking about it, it sounded like suicide.

"In Ancient Times, you broke my Absolute Defense, and now you’ve pierced through my black mist. Immortal, you really are tough to deal with."

Yao Saint’s tone carried a hint of resentment, as if by some twist of fate, such events were constantly being replayed.

As a user of ’Speak and Follow,’ he had countless attempts on his life along the way. How could he not use ’Speak and Follow’ to increase his defenses—but to his surprise, the Immortal Fairy proved so powerful that she shattered the Absolute Defense he had cast with ’Speak and Follow.’

In preparation to battle the Time Immortal who had yet to ascend to immortality, his Absolute Defense was strong enough to withstand attacks of time itself. Besides that, it could also withstand all sorts of attacks, including spatial curses. However, despite his thorough preparations, Immortal Fairy broke through with pure strength.

It was absolutely unbelievable. Were all geniuses from other star systems this powerful?

He had long utilized ’Speak and Follow’ to set a life-saving measure for himself that could help him feign death and escape, anticipating such a situation.

From this encounter, he realized that there were always stronger beings, and he chose to bide his time, feigning death as if he never existed.

"Immortal, you took advantage of my unpreparedness to launch a surprise attack against me, an uncharitable victory, and yet you dare question why I would want to kill you?"

"It was you who first obliterated an innocent tribe!" Immortal Fairy exclaimed angrily, recalling the time when Yao Saint sought to destroy a small tribe, and she had no choice but to intervene urgently.

Moreover, she could only resort to a surprise attack, she and Yao Saint both being at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage; if they were to do battle, that tribe would surely suffer the consequences.

The tribe she belonged to had perished because of the clash of two mighty beings, leaving only her alive. The battle had even inadvertently affected them, and she was determined to prevent such a tragedy from occurring again.

"Mortals fail to recognize celestial authority, offend me, how could they expect anything other than death?" Yao Saint said coldly.

Born high above others, mortals were nothing but playthings to amuse him, even cultivators in his eyes were merely larger playthings. If these playthings did not obey him, killing them was of no concern.

"How did Yao Saint secretly become an immortal, using Verbal Spell to block my probing?" Yingtian Immortal murmured to himself, still puzzled.

His Tribulation Dao Fruit controlled the Heavenly Tribulation, and the Immortal Ascension Tribulation could not possibly be concealed from his Tribulation Dao Fruit.

This meant Yao Saint must have ascended to immortality before him.

But that’s not right, Verbal Spell is a divine ability, not a Dao Fruit Outline, and a divine ability could not possibly deceive the outline of his Tribulation Dao Fruit.

Unless...

Yingtian Immortal quickly realized, "His Dao Fruit is Verbal Spell!"

Only by elevating Verbal Spell to the level of a Speak and Follow Dao Fruit Outline, could he deceive his own Tribulation Dao Fruit Outline and ascend to immortality in secret!

The Speak and Follow Dao Fruit, this is an unfamiliar Dao Fruit to all, its true capabilities unknown to anyone!

"Quite lively here," a rather familiar voice suddenly rang out beside Lu Yang.

Lu Yang turned to see, it was Jiang Pingan, disguised as an old farmer, nondescript at all, so he quickly paid his respects, "So it’s the elder Jiang Pingan, what brings you here?"

Jiang Pingan looked at Lu Yang intently. Nonsense, such a commotion on my turf, almost piercing through the world, could I not come?

Do you really think you own the whole world just because you’re protected by Daoist Yun Zhi and Daoist Immortal?

And without my permission, how could Yun Zhi possibly use the Power of National Fate so freely? Do you think my Power of National Fate is for everyone to borrow?

To prevent Yao Saint from escaping, Jiang Pingan had Yun Zhi mobilize the entire Power of National Fate of Great Xia.

Lu Yang thought for a moment; it seemed he had never seen Jiang Pingan make a move. "Now that you’re here, why don’t you demonstrate some of your skills?"

Jiang Pingan gave Lu Yang an unimpressed look. This young man never had good intentions. He had arrived during the battle between Fairy Eternity and Yao Saint, a battle he certainly was not qualified to join.

"Let’s not. My old bones can’t stand such disturbance, and my Dao Fruit isn’t suited for battle."

"Daoist Yun Zhi asked me to come to your side, to keep an eye on the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, to prevent him from causing trouble."

Yun Zhi knew it would be difficult for Lu Yang alone to watch over the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, so she called for help.

Jiang Pingan, smiling, looked at the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, "But it seems he’s quite docile."

"Daoist Mo Qingshui has established the Great Qian Dynasty atop the ruins, I’ve long heard of your name, and you should have heard of me. This is, after all, our first meeting."

"Scram!"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord cursed rudely, although there wasn’t any actual grievance between them. Yet, both being Founding Emperors, one captured and the other exalted, this contrast made him loathe the sight of Jiang Pingan.

Jiang Pingan wasn’t a petty man; after being cursed, he still spoke politely, "Daoist Mo, why be so hasty? I heard you’ve been seeking the Four Ancient Immortals, even threatening to dispose of them if they don’t cooperate, to replace them with your four Divine Monarchs. Today, three of the Four Ancient Immortals are gathered. Aren’t you going to meet them, or should I call them down for you?"

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord went silent for a moment, then gave a bowed greeting, "Daoist Jiang Pingan, who swept across the land to establish Great Xia, forging extraordinary merits, I’ve long admired your name."

Chapter 1251: Chapter 1250 Speak and Follow Dao Fruit

"Has it been long enough for the battle to be over?"

Based on experience, after such a long time, the matter should have been resolved.

Meng Jingzhou stealthily opened the exit of Fengdu Space, peeked out half of his face, and felt the crushing aura of the Desolate Ancient hit him, leaving him gasping for air.

When he saw the situation outside, he instinctively took a sharp intake of breath.

Eldest Senior Sister’s face, rich with expressions, was engaged in a duel with a formidable enemy, wreaking havoc. The Qilin Immortal, Yingtian Immortal, and Immortal Jiuchong, three immortals, were idly floating and watching, while Old Lu stood beside Jiang Pingan and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord.

Such a gathering had never been seen before throughout ancient and modern times; immortals are mysterious and unpredictable, yet today they appeared in droves.

Even the watching immortals numbered five!

The formidable enemy’s background was unknown, but he was managing to go toe-to-toe with Eldest Senior Sister, and the five immortals spectating had no opportunity to intervene.

Meng Jingzhou silently withdrew his head.

"What’s it like out there?" Man Gu asked anxiously.

Meng Jingzhou patted Man Gu’s shoulder, his face expressing immense relief as he delivered good news to County Magistrate Man, "The first Immortal Battle is happening outside, and Zhongshan County ruins are certain to become a famous historic site."

...

To call this battle the first Immortal Battle wasn’t an exaggeration on Meng Jingzhou’s part – Fairy Eternity was using Yun Zhi’s body to duel with Yao Saint, and even the Yingtian Four Immortals from Ancient Times hadn’t caused such a dramatic collision when they jointly battled against Yao Saint.

If not for the protective barrier, by this moment the entire Cultivation World would be enveloped in overwhelming might.

Previously, Fairy Eternity’s battle with Ashy Bean completely disregarded distance, the battlefield spanning billions of miles, stretching from the Demon Territory to the Land of No Spirit, showing how frightening such a high-level battle could be.

It was only Great Xia’s accumulation of State Destiny over a hundred thousand years that was strong enough to build a barrier capable of preventing the leakage of power. If it were up to Yingtian Immortal’s crafted items like the Qiankun Cover, it would definitely be impossible to achieve such an effect.

The barrier enveloped Zhongshan County, meaning the astonishing power of the first Immortal Battle was squeezed entirely into this place, filling the whole space.

Space trembled, and Lu Yang noticed ripples continuously forming on his skin, resonating with the space, beyond his control, forcing him to shake along with it.

Lu Yang’s case was not unique; whether it was the Yingtian Three Immortals in the sky or the two Founding Emperors on the ground, they all faced similar situations. Under spatial resonance, even talking and transmitting Spiritual Sense became extremely difficult.

Jiang Pingan and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s friendly conversation was also abruptly halted.

Now that he knew his own abilities, Yao Saint no longer concealed them, choosing to fight with all his might.

Speak and summon; define the Rule!

When battling with the Four Ancient Immortals, he had always recited the [Rule] in his heart, so it was difficult for the Four Immortals to guess his true abilities, only finding him enigmatic.

Speak and summon, since there is a "speak" in it, it indicates that to fully unleash the power of the Dao Fruit, the most important thing is to say it aloud.

And the pressure that Immortal gave him forced him to stop holding back!

"[Thou shalt lose consciousness]"

Upon these words, Immortal Fairy indeed lost consciousness and suddenly stopped her attacking motions, frozen in place!

Seeing this, Yao Saint decisively struck, his Fist technique also incredibly exquisite, Chaotic Light surging, Ancient Phenomenon occurring frequently, ancestral worship, Demon God shrieking, demons emerging!

These were the innate phenomena accompanying his birth!

The main reason he spoke so spitefully toward Qilin Immortal was that he was the true chosen one by destiny!

Born with phenomena, mastering Speak and Follow, his words could decide the life and death of others, the direction of tribes, everywhere his star system held him as divine!

His Fist technique was overwhelmingly powerful, with boundless Mana.

Yet this punch, when it landed on Immortal Fairy, couldn’t harm her in the slightest!

What was happening? Was it because the body she was using was too strong, or was this one of the abilities of the Eternity Dao Fruit?

Reality didn’t give Yao Saint the opportunity to think, as Fairy Eternity suddenly opened her eyes, her gaze shimmering brilliantly.

"To think that I would fall into the Heart Devil Tribulation!"

Fairy Eternity hadn’t lost consciousness directly but was caught in the Heart Devil Tribulation, unable to extricate herself for a full five breaths’ time!

Fairy Eternity grabbed Yao Saint’s wrist with a fist like rolling thunder, swift as lightning, striking decisively!

"Do you think I would fear you?"

Yao Saint’s black mist was just one of many defensive measures; his physical body was equally terrifyingly strong.

He had often reflected on why he had been defeated by Fairy Eternity in ancient times, deducing it was because he had been overly protected by "Speak and Follow," lacking in personal hardship.

For this reason, he had become an ascetic monk, studying the ways of physical tempering; his body had become incomparably tough!

The two continuously exchanged blows, with the fallout reaching the barrier, causing continuous ripples that pained Jiang Pingan to watch.

Fairy Eternity was like a blazing inferno, fiercely burning in combat, consuming her enemies.

Yao Saint was calm and collected as the eternal profound ice, analyzing Fairy Eternity’s fist techniques, contemplating his next move.

Immortal battles changed in the blink of an eye; within a few breaths, they’d clashed thousands of times, and Yao Saint found that Fairy Eternity’s techniques were completely erratic, impossible to predict.

She was actually fighting solely on instinct!

Neither Fairy Eternity nor Yao Saint understood each other’s combat style. Fairy Eternity, since becoming an immortal, rarely engaged in combat, and even when she did, it was only to spar with the Yingtian Four Immortals, hardly enough to reveal her true combat style!

Yao Saint was the first to falter in his techniques, mistaking a movement and giving Fairy Eternity an opening!

Fairy Eternity aimed for Yao Saint’s gap and threw a punch, while Yao Saint coldly issued a command.

"Immune."

Out of nowhere, countless pieces of Immortal Gold appeared, forming armor around Yao Saint’s body, with even more at the targeted spot.

Boom!

Her punch landed squarely and solidly on the reinforced Immortal Gold Armor; Fairy Eternity had hoped to use a force transference technique to hit Yao Saint through the armor.

However, the suit of Immortal Gold Armor was made of multiple layers of Immortal Gold with gaps between each layer, so the force couldn’t reach Yao Saint at all!

Fairy Eternity’s eyes were bright as snow, and a thought flashed through her mind.

The Speak and Follow Dao Fruit didn’t create rules directly but worked in other ways to fulfill Yao Saint’s commands.

If that were the case, then there was still a fight to be had!

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord watching the battle was stunned. Although it was Fairy Eternity using Yun Zhi’s body, one couldn’t gauge Yun Zhi’s true strength through this fight. Yet, such combat prowess indicated just how powerful Yun Zhi was, as Fairy Eternity extravagantly expended power without damaging her own body.

Any other immortal would undoubtedly not be able to withstand such force.

Yun Zhi’s power far exceeded his predictions.

And that Fairy Eternity, equally terrifying.

With these two presiding over Seek Dao Sect, had he really considered attacking them before?!

Was I tired of living?

"Time Stop."

Yao Saint once again gave a command, and all of Zhongshan County fell into a state of temporal stasis. Everything halted—the rippling barrier, the trembling and twisting space, the gravel floating in mid-air, the expressions of the various onlookers...

And Fairy Eternity, who was completely unaffected by it!

The Eternity Dao Fruit, unchanging and constant, unaffected by time, uneroded by the years.

Chapter 1252: Chapter 1251: You Can Self-Detonate Using Someone Else’s Body?!

"Hundred Grass Withering Fist!"

All grass withered, trees wilted, and Yao Saint’s body deflated like a punctured balloon, his vitality rapidly escaping. Even with the seemingly limitless lifespan of an Immortal, he could not withstand such a swift drain of vitality; if it continued, he might fall into the Heavenly Person Five Decays!

"[Vitality Stabilization]."

Yao Saint once again used his Verbal Spell, and the fast-depleting vitality came to an abrupt halt, replenishing what was lost from his body.

Time flowed once again, returning to normal.

"Did time just stop?"

After Yao Saint ordered time to stop, Lu Yang lost consciousness.

And certainly, Immortal Fairy and Eldest Senior Sister should not be capable of making time flow again.

The only one who could do that was Yao Saint.

If time stopped, why would Yao Saint want time to flow again?

"It seems that a later Verbal Spell can override an earlier one, or perhaps the burden of sustaining two simultaneous commands is too much for Yao Saint to bear?"

Lu Yang analyzed the situation and concluded that the Speak and Follow Dao Fruit was not invincible. First off, Yao Saint couldn’t simply order effects like "[Conquer Immortal Fairy][Open Box World]"; secondly, the Verbal Spell didn’t directly set rules but relied on other means to achieve its purpose; and lastly, there could only be one active [Rule] at any given moment for Yao Saint in the same space-time.

That being said, the Speak and Follow Dao Fruit was still astonishingly against the natural order. Considering the few commands Yao Saint had issued, it was as if he had access to all the powers of Dao Fruits, which is why even the four Ancient Immortals together could not defeat him.

From this perspective, altering the timeline was also an effect of Yao Saint using the Speak and Follow Dao Fruit.

"[You are abandoned by the Five Elements]."

Yao Saint issued another command, Lu Yang saw the ground beneath him transformed into the Soil of Rest, more precious even than the Soil of Rest found in the Seek Dao Sect’s Medicine Garden, being the legendary Nine Heavens Breath Soil.

The Breath Soil loosened, seedlings sprouted, and in the blink of an eye turned into a colossal tree reaching into the sky!

"The Jianmu Tree?!"

The Yingtian Immortals exclaimed in shock; the tree that had broken through the soil was actually the Time Immortal’s former self, the Jianmu Tree?

The physical form of Time Immortal was the heavenly-reaching Firmament Tree, and among many sentient plants, Time Immortal managed to achieve the status of an Immortal and comprehend the Time Dao Fruit, which was closely related to the Jianmu Tree.

That alone illustrated the miraculous nature of Jianmu, so much so that calling it an Immortal Tree was no exaggeration.

And in the world, there was only one Jianmu belonging to Time Immortal.

And now, Yao Saint, through the power of Verbal Spell, had conjured another Jianmu Tree!

Subsequently, a nondescript river appeared on the ground, the Weak Water River, where nothing sinks, a natural sealing material.

And when Nine Heavens Breath Soil encounters water, it swells, absorbing the Weak Water River, rapidly expanding, it also has sealing capabilities!

The Jianmu Tree grew wildly, entwining around Immortal Fairy. As she tried to break free, the swelling Nine Heavens Breath Soil crept along the Jianmu Tree upwards, sealing Immortal Fairy firmly in place, allowing only her head to show.

Immortal Fairy struggled with all her might but found the seal made from Jianmu and Nine Heavens Breath Soil to be incredibly robust, proving impossible to break free!

Then, Heavenly Fire descended, incinerating all, and the essence of the Five Elements materialized out of thin air, evolving into various Immortal Artifacts, Treasure Tripods, Gourds, Palm Fans, Jade Flutes...

Those abandoned by the Five Elements were to be executed by the Five Elements.

The expressions of Yingtian Immortals and the others drastically changed at the sight; Immortal Fairy could not avoid the attack, forced to withstand the Heavenly Fire and the Immortal Artifacts formed from the essence of the Five Elements.

No matter how powerful an Immortal, it was impossible to block this attack!

Yingtian Immortal directed Thunder Tribulation to shatter the Immortal Artifacts, which turned out to be single-use and not as durable as expected.

The Immortal Jiuchong played the world like a chessboard, defining Heavenly Fire as "Yang," and used "Yin" chess pieces to counter the Heavenly Fire.

The Qilin Immortal transformed back into its original form, roaring within the cosmos, striking at the roots of the Jianmu Tree!

While the Immortal Artifacts and Heavenly Fire continued to disappear, they also kept emerging, with no end in sight. The roots of Jianmu protected by the Nine Heavens Breath Soil, as soon as the Qilin Immortal touched the Breath Soil, the soil and the tree began to grow onto him, intending to seal him along with the rest.

Eventually, the Heavenly Fire descended, the Immortal Artifacts exploded, and the booming noise never ceased, with smoke billowing everywhere!

Suddenly, out of the smoke, an irresistible force burst forth, scattering the smoke, and the Jianmu and Breath Soil exploded, scattering fragments all around!

Fairy Eternity moved her limbs, emitting creaking noises all over, and revealed an extremely content expression.

"At last, I have fully adapted to Miss Yun’s body. Your body was truly difficult to get used to!"

"Fairy Eternity, you flatter me."

Since her revival, Fairy Eternity had never felt as comfortable as at that moment, not even when she battled with Ashy Bean and conjured her Immortal Body, which wasn’t as comfortable as Miss Yun’s body.

Finally, she could exert her full strength!

"[Bluffing]."

As the Verbal Spell was activated, Fairy Eternity underwent no change.

Yao Saint’s face turned somewhat ugly.

"Yao Saint, it seems like your Verbal Spell can’t be used directly on me! Let’s go again!"

"Since you were unsatisfied with your own suicide last time, this time I’ll beat you to death!"

Fully adapted to her new body, Fairy Eternity’s spirit shone brightly, her Qi and Blood soared to the skies, and her entire being glowed. Her dark, elegant hair fluttered with her Qi and Blood, displaying a dashing and heroic spirit. She exuded a self-assured beauty that seemed to declare her the unmatched hero of heaven and earth.

Lu Yang was suddenly moved.

The gold Immortal Fist rained down like a storm, unrestrained and domineering, each punch filled with murderous intent. Yao Saint, too, erupted with a horrifying aura, his power permeating the air, a match for Fairy Eternity’s edge!

Amid the flow of Qi, Blood, and immortal power, the battle became hard to discern.

The heavens shattered and the earth cracked as both Qi, Blood, and immortal power dispersed!

Fairy Eternity was all offense and no defense, forcing Yao Saint to repeatedly retreat and leaving him no chance to even utter his Verbal Spell!

Yao Saint once again entertained the thought of retreat, but what welcomed him was Fairy Eternity’s even sharper fists!

Fairy Eternity, unrivaled and supreme!

Fairy Eternity shone with a dazzling brilliance, like a stunningly beautiful fairy from ancient legends unparallel in elegance!

She took a deep breath and launched the strongest attack since the battle began! freewebnøvel.coɱ

Boom!

Crack!

Yao Saint’s spine exploded inch by inch, broken bones piercing his body, causing unbearable pain!

"That feels better."

Fairy Eternity took a long breath and wiped the sweat from her forehead, releasing all her resentment for Yao Saint through her punches.

She grinned and said, "Now it’s time to get serious!"

Fairy Eternity became increasingly radiant; or rather, Miss Yun’s body became increasingly radiant, shining like the brilliant sun.

Apart from Jiang Pingan and Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, those present were all too familiar with Fairy Eternity’s state.

She was going to self-detonate!

"Why are you reacting like this?" Jiang Pingan didn’t understand why Lu Yang’s expression had drastically changed.

Lu Yang had no time for lengthy explanations and quickly pulled Jiang Pingan and Mid-heaven Emperor Lord into the Green Blade Sword Small World.

The Yingtian Three Immortals also rushed headlong into the Green Blade Sword Small World.

Having entered the Green Blade Sword Small World, the Yingtian Immortal even took out several Immortal Artifacts containing small world spaces and threw them outside the Green Blade Sword, wrapping it up.

Those in the know were finally able to breathe a sigh of relief within the layers of small worlds.

For the first time in his life, Yao Saint showed an expression of disbelief.

You can self-detonate using someone else’s body?!

What awaited Yao Saint was the most powerful explosion in history.

Boom——

Chapter 1253: Chapter 1252: Reduced to Ashes

The Immortal Artifacts that were placed around the Green Peak Sword had all been meticulously crafted by the Yingtian Immortal, and he felt his own Immortal Artifacts breaking apart layer by layer.

Even the innermost Green Blade Sword Small World was shaking violently as if there were an earth-shattering event taking place.

Jiang Pingan could feel that the barrier he created using the Power of National Fate was being battered mercilessly, a horrible sight to behold.

The spherical barrier twisted under the impact of the self-detonation, stretching upwards and downwards as if it were dough being kneaded ruthlessly on a board.

Jiang Pingan and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord watched with pounding hearts, finally understanding why the others had reacted so strongly before.

Those who were slow to escape would follow in Yao Saint’s footsteps.

Within the barrier, only Yao Saint was left, covered in wounds, vomiting Immortal Blood, his Immortal Gold Armor blasted into pieces during the self-detonation, fragments embedding into his flesh—an injury severity he hadn’t experienced since Ancient Times.

But he ultimately held out.

Next, he saw Yun Zhi’s body, which after the self-detonation hovered in mid-air before the blood mist recondensed, the Fairy Eternity as radiant as ever, not having felt this exhilarated by self-detonation in ages.

Yun Zhi’s expression was somewhat odd; this was the first time she had ever experienced the taste of self-detonation, which was embarrassingly humiliating.

Had she known it would be like this, she would have preferred not to borrow a body and dealt with Yao Saint personally.

Before Fairy Eternity prepared for a second round of self-detonation, she glanced down at the lonely Green Peak Sword stuck in the ground.

As for the scattered remnants of Immortal Artifacts by the sword’s side, she automatically deemed them insignificant.

"Grant the Green Peak Sword an Immortal status."

This was a Rule she had imbued before her self-detonation.

The Fengdu Space and the barrier had also been granted Immortal status by her.

"Let’s go again!"

Since she had already vented enough with her fists, she might as well finish things off cleanly!

The Immortal Fairy burst forth with a dazzling glow for the second self-detonation, the speed of which left Yao Saint no chance to even utter the Verbal Spell; he could only recite it silently in his heart.

"Absolute Defense."

Black fog condensed, Immortal Gold layer upon layer wrapping Yao Saint tightly.

But it was futile.

The second self-detonation dispersed the black fog, tore through the Immortal Gold, blasting Yao Saint’s Immortal Body full of holes.

The people in the Green Blade Sword Small World were astonished, not because Yao Saint couldn’t withstand the self-detonation, but because they couldn’t understand why the Green Peak Sword remained unscathed amidst it all?!

The first wave of self-detonation had destroyed no less than three spatial-type Immortal Artifacts!

"Is Wu Yao’s Artifact Refining Technique even better than mine?"

The Yingtian Immortal, renowned as the Ancestor of Refining, was dealt a blow, his own techniques seemingly inferior to those of a later generation Immortal.

"You are abandoned by the Five Elements."

The Nine Heavens Breath Soil, the Firmament Tree, the Ruishui River, the Heavenly Fire, the Five Elements Essence—all reappeared, this time aiming to completely seal the Immortal Fairy.

Unfortunately, in the face of absolute power, even to attack was wishful thinking.

These Five Elements Immortal Objects had just emerged, and before they could show their power, they were obliterated by the self-detonation into nothingness, their Immortal essence lost completely.

"Rejuvenation."

The words in Yao Saint’s heart were equivalent to possessing the Revitalizing Tao Fruit, his injuries quickly healing.

But no matter how fast he healed, he couldn’t outpace the speed of Immortal Fairy’s self-detonation!

"Has the self-detonation stopped?"

During the self-detonation, none dared to probe out with their Immortal Sense from within the Green Blade Sword Small World, for in such a state, any Immortal Sense venturing out would be shattered, seeing nothing.

Now that the Green Peak Sword had stopped trembling, everyone probed out with their Spiritual Sense.

They saw Yao Saint not only blasted to the point his Immortal Body was gone, but even his Three Souls and Seven Spirits and his foundational core severely damaged, like a deflated sack, shriveled and feeble.

"Immortal, good, you’re quite good!"

Yao Saint clenched his teeth, his expression brimming with resentment.

He had utterly lost this battle. Was it because Immortal had been in some strange state before that allowed him to successfully ambush her?

But things were not over yet.

"Immortal, don’t think you’re the only one who can self-detonate!"

Yao Saint’s body also lit up, exactly like Fairy Eternity’s a moment ago, clearly intending to self-detonate!

"Bad, he’s trying to escape!" Lu Yang realized, and quickly shouted.

Since Yao Saint had been able to feign death to escape through Verbal Spell during his Transcendence Tribulation Stage, then as an Immortal, he must be capable of the same feat!

Lu Yang even suspected that Yao Saint could maintain two Verbal Spells at the same time in the same space, one of them being the ongoing feigned death for escape!

Yao Saint laughed heartily, knowing his tactics, what could they do about it? Did they have any countermeasures?

"With such a vast world, where can’t I go? To catch me, the only way is for Yun Zhi to actively pursue Harmonization!"

"Yun Zhi, dare you harmonize?"

Either he would self-detonate and escape, or Yun Zhi would pay the price of Harmonization, become Heaven itself, and track down his whereabouts!

Yun Zhi’s disdainful attitude towards him angered him. Did she really think he was so easily manipulated?

Faced with a dilemma, he wanted to see how she would choose!

Yun Zhi remained indifferent towards Yao Saint, silent and calm; she had discussed how to deal with such situations with Fairy Eternity during battle.

Just then, Fairy Eternity suddenly pulled out a hoe from behind and struck at Yao Saint’s head, leaving only a shallow imprint.

However, Yao Saint showed a terrified expression: "This, this is..."

The hoe was utterly ordinary, without any unique features, resembling one used by farmers.

Coincidentally, Lu Yang had seen this hoe before, and its owner was standing right beside him.

Lu Yang turned his head towards Jiang Pingan: "Is that the hoe you often use?"

The farmer-like Jiang Pingan chuckled: "This is not a hoe; this is the Taishang Sword."

"The Taishang Sword!?"

Lu Yang suddenly remembered, at the Qingzhou celebration, when Great Yu’s Pass Tribulation Cultivator attacked, the Qingzhou Governor used the Illusory Shadow of the Taishang Sword, which directly rendered the rules of Great Yu’s Pass Tribulation Cultivator ineffective.

If the Illusory Shadow of the Taishang Sword held such power, could it be that...

"The true ability of the Taishang Sword is to render the Dao Fruit ineffective!?"

Jiang Pingan humbly smiled: "It’s not quite that exaggerated. It depends on the strength of the opponent—the stronger the opponent, the shorter the duration of ineffectiveness. This Yao Saint is so powerful, I estimate it can only render him ineffective for five seconds."

Lu Yang glanced sideways, knowing that in Immortal combat, a moment’s difference in timing could determine victory or defeat.

To render the Dao Fruit ineffective for five seconds was indeed terrifying.

Jiang Pingan indeed was not skilled in combat, even with the Taishang Sword in hand, which was why he preferred to lend the Taishang Sword to those skilled in Immortal combat.

"But why does the Taishang Sword take the form of a hoe?" Lu Yang asked. If not for the hoe being effective, he would never have associated it with the Taishang Sword.

The other Immortals also wanted to know the reason.

Jiang Pingan rolled his eyes; it was a simple question: "Everyone knows my Taishang Sword is dangerous, so if I were to reveal it, wouldn’t the enemy be warned?"

The door creaked open slightly, and Lu Yang stuck his head out, "Nothing serious, just an Immortal Battle breaking out."

"Huh?"

Through the crack, Ming Yu the Abbot saw two strangers fighting with a kirin, incense burners and offering plates flying everywhere, with Time Immortal just standing by, making no attempt to break up the fight.

These incense burners and offering plates, having been purified by incense smoke over time, were no different in quality from Immortal Artifacts.

Ming Yu, the Abbot, felt that although he was a few thousand years older than Lu Yang, when it came to knowledge, he was far behind Lu Yang, who showed no surprise at the scene.

Lu Yang closed the door again.

The three Immortals formed a tripartite standoff, Kirin Immortal holding a writing desk, Yingtian Immortal carrying an incense burner, and Immortal Jiuchong carrying an offering plate, while Lu Yang munched on the offerings.

Kirin Immortal, wary of Yingtian Immortal and Immortal Jiuchong, suddenly burst into laughter, tears streaming down his face.

The others were infected by his laughter and joined in heartily.

Kirin Immortal, still laughing, waved his hands, doubling over with laughter and eventually laying down, "Okay, okay, I’m done fighting, you guys can hit me however you like."

Yingtian Immortal and Immortal Jiuchong lay on the ground, exhausted, "Pssh, as if we want to hit you."

Time Immortal, as the eldest brother, initially wanted to maintain some dignity by sitting, but seeing his brothers lying down, he too laid down on the ground directly.

With the misunderstanding cleared, the Four Ancient Immortals were reunited, lying on the ground, feeling that the flow of time was peaceful.

They had waited for this day for three hundred thousand years, it had been too long, far too long.

Fairy Eternity also felt it was not easy for everyone to be together, "Since it’s rare for all of us to gather, how about I show you my skills and make something you all love to eat?"

The words of Fairy Eternity brought them back to reality, scaring the Four Ancient Immortals into sitting up and saying there was no need.

Chapter 1258: Chapter 1257: How Did Elder Brother Dai Take Sick Leave?

"Immortal Fairy, you just went through a battle, you must be very tired, don’t worry about it anymore."

"Ah? But I’m not tired yet..."

"We appreciate the thought, Immortal Fairy, please rest well."

"After all, Buddha Country is my territory, how could I let a guest cook? Fortunately, I have some offerings here..."

While speaking, Lu Yang picked up the last piece of cake, but when he saw Time Immortal looking at him, he guiltily put it back.

Earlier, while watching the battle among the three immortals, Lu Yang had enjoyed it while eating and watching.

Time Immortal: "..."

You really don’t see yourself as an outsider!

"I will have food prepared right away."

Time Immortal contacted Ming Yu through a mental message, asking him to bring out fine Spirit Food to celebrate.

Soon, various mushy dishes were laid in front of everyone, bubbling continuously, clearly freshly made.

Yingtian Immortal and the others silently looked at Time Immortal, what kind of stuff are you serving us?

Embarrassed, Time Immortal coughed twice and contacted Ming Yu again, I told you to bring Spirit Fruit cakes and the like, not these.

Fortunately, the atmosphere among the people gathered was the most important, not the food, so the harmony was quickly restored.

The Five Ancient Immortals reminisced about the past, laughing continuously, and influenced by the cheerful atmosphere, Lu Yang also laughed, occasionally chipping in a few words.

Immortal Jiuchong grew suspicious, "Little Friend Lu seems to be very familiar with our experiences in ancient times?"

Before Lu Yang could respond, Immortal Fairy proudly stepped forward and said, "Of course, I’ve told Little Yang everything about our ancient times!"

"For example, Jiuchong, in order to make people remember you were the first to become an immortal, spent massive amounts of Heaven and Earth Treasures to create a celestial phenomenon during your Crossing the Immortal Tribulation."

"Like Time, you asked me which among the world’s heroes could become immortals, criticizing everyone, claiming you were the first to achieve immortality and then you got beaten up."

"Like Qilin, the sword array you knelt on that softened upon touch was crafted by Yingtian Immortal."

Immortal Fairy counted on her fingers as she recalled what she had told Lu Yang, and with every incident, one person’s expression dramatically changed.

Only Yingtian Immortal remained unperturbed and unfazed.

Lu Yang suddenly felt the once merry atmosphere had somewhat shifted.

Time Immortal stood up, approached Lu Yang with a chuckle, "Little Friend Lu, reviving Immortal Fairy is indeed a great merit, let me toast to you."

There’s no wine in Western Paradise Temple, so Time Immortal was holding a bowl of mush.

Although it was a gesture of thanks, Lu Yang found Time Immortal’s gaze somewhat menacing.

"Little Friend Lu, I toast to you as well."

"I toast too."

Immortal Jiuchong and Qilin Immortal got up one after another, taking turns toasting Lu Yang with mush, which made Lu Yang’s hands tremble as he held his bowl.

Fortunately, Yingtian Immortal had already reckoned with Lu Yang and was no longer holding a grudge, kindly diverting the topic, "By the way, Little Friend Lu, have you encountered anything interesting outside of Box World?"

"Yes, yes, tell us, what is it like outside Box World now?"

The others were also very curious.

Lu Yang’s expression was a bit odd, "It’s not exactly fun, initially I was just going to the hospital, seeing the doctor... and encountered a zombie crisis... Later, I found that the crisis was orchestrated by a place called Candle Sky Civilization..."

Lu Yang honestly shared his experiences before coming to the Box World, and the immortals listened with great interest, finding the outside world very different from what they had imagined.

"Should we undo the seal and open the box?" Immortal Jiuchong suggested.

They refined stars into continents to resurrect Fairy Eternity and to prevent the hidden hand from escaping.

Now that Fairy Eternity had been resurrected and Yao Saint had been executed, there was no need to continue the seal.

Having come from ancient times, they knew how vast the starry sky was, but the people of the Box World did not know; this was an opportunity to show them the real starry sky.

And they had thought that when they set the seal, they had gathered all beings in the universe. According to what Lu Yang had said, there were still beings outside, probably in remote areas that were not included in the collection range.

"Sure, I have no objections."

"I agree."

"I agree too."

The Four Ancient Immortals each stated their position,

"It’s great. Once we’re out, let’s help Little Yang find his original planet and by the way, look for my North Star," said Fairy Eternity cheerfully.

In fact, the Mid-Heaven Emperor Lord had always misunderstood the seal. Unsealing it required the joint efforts not just of the Four Ancient Immortals but of the Five Ancient Immortals.

Lu Yang felt a tingling in his heart; he wanted to see the outside world too. When he first came to the Cultivation World, he thought he would never see his past life again. Since there was no chance, he stopped thinking about his past life and enjoyed this hard-won life.

Who would have known that just outside the Box World was his own world, and there were many things there he still cared about, like how Blue Star and the Candle Sky Civilization were doing.

"However, since it involves completely unsealing, it’s not urgent at this moment; there’s still a lot of preparation to be done."

Lu Yang spoke seriously. Although he wanted to visit the outside world, such matters could not be rushed.

Unsealing and opening the Box World would be a significant upheaval for the entire Cultivation World, especially for those cultivators who could traverse the cosmos. Great Xia might be manageable since various cultivators there tended to follow rules, but not those from Buddhism, the Demon Territory, or the East Sea; cultivators and demons there would swarm out upon hearing this news.

Approaches to publicity, response plans, behavior norms, etc., all needed to be considered.

Let’s not talk about remote concerns; one could not simply sit down, have a meal, and decide to unseal, then unseal after finishing the meal.

At the very least, they needed to give advanced notice to Eldest Senior Sister, Jiang Pingan, and others.

"That makes sense, let’s take it one step at a time," the Immortals such as Yingtian Immortal laughed, as they were not short of time.

As everyone had almost finished eating, Fairy Eternity asked, "What are your plans? Do you want to come visit our Seek Dao Sect?"

"Sure."

Yingtian Immortal and Immortal Jiuchong had visited the Seek Dao Sect before, and Time Immortal had also hurried over once to look for Fairy Eternity and Yun Zhi after the timeline changed. Qilin Immortal, however, had never visited.

Before leaving Western Paradise Temple, Lu Yang visited Xin Ding; Xin Ding was very suited to Buddhism, progressing step by step in cultivation and had already made a great name in Buddha Country. Lu Yang felt that given Xin Ding’s talents, it would not be a problem for him to become the new Abbot in time.

He then left with peace of mind.

A group of six, including five Immortals and one in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage—rounded up, that’s six Immortals.

Six Immortals traveling together reached unparalleled speeds and soon arrived at the Seek Dao Sect.

"Elder Brother Dai, I’ve brought a few guests to visit our Sect..."

Lu Yang confidently went to the Task Hall and pushed open the door to Dai Bufan’s room, only to find it empty.

Upon inquiring, he learned that Dai Bufan had taken sick leave, which Lu Yang regretted, as having the Four Ancient Immortals visit the Seek Dao Sect was a magnificent event. How could Elder Brother Dai miss out on such fortune?

He had no choice but to take the Five Ancient Immortals to Sky Gate Mountain to find Eldest Senior Sister.

"Eldest Senior Sister, I heard Elder Brother Dai is on sick leave. What happened to him? I’d like to visit him."

Yun Zhi raised her eyelids, also puzzled.

"He’s sick? He was fine when I spoke to him just now."

"What did you talk about with him?"

"Nothing much, just that Jiuyou Sect and Yaoyang Sect surrendered to Junior Brother Man. I’ve captured the Mid-Heaven Emperor Lord. The Four Ancient Immortals refined stars into continents to deal with Yao Saint, and I helped the Ancient Immortals handle Yao Saint. The Four Ancient Immortals should be visiting our Sect soon, so I told him to prepare."

Yun Zhi thought for a moment, "That’s it, just these things."

Chapter 1259: Chapter 1258: I, the Lonely Qilin Immortal

"Junior Brother Dai must be exhausted from long-term work, both mentally and physically. It would be good for him to rest for a while. You should not visit him, Junior Brother. Let him recuperate peacefully."

Lu Yang really wanted to say, "Could it be, Eldest Senior Sister, that you scared Elder Brother Dai?"

Even Lu Yang knew how astonishing the series of events was, so he had originally planned to only share the news of the Four Ancient Immortals visiting with Elder Brother Dai, and not discuss anything else.

Unexpectedly, Eldest Senior Sister told him everything.

"Esteemed predecessors are here to visit the Seek Dao Sect, welcome." Yun Zhi greeted each of the Four Ancient Immortals, who were so frightened that they kept returning the greetings. Three-quarters of them had been disciplined by Yun Zhi before.

Even the remaining Qilin Immortal had seen Yun Zhi displaying her power in Zhongshan County.

"However, I need to go to Imperial City to see Mr. Jiang. How about letting Fairy Senior and Junior Brother lead you on the tour?"

"No worries at all," the Four Ancient Immortals quickly replied, as Yun Zhi’s nonchalant demeanor oppressed them from daring to enjoy themselves.

"What are you going to do in Imperial City?" Fairy Eternity wondered, still considering having Miss Yun guide them through the Seek Dao Sect.

Besides, hadn’t she just met Jiang Ping’an in Zhongshan County?

Yun Zhi sighed faintly, a rare occurrence, "After the battle in Imperial City, Guan Shanhai’s Three Souls and Seven Spirits, physical body, and Dao Fruit were all separated. Our Seek Dao Sect kept the Three Souls and Dao Fruit, while the Dynasty kept the Seven Spirits and the physical body."

Lu Yang nodded. He, of course, remembered this—it was his idea.

"Guan Shanhai just mentioned that he feels powerless and restricted in Captive Peak and wants to retrieve his Seven Spirits and physical body. I’ll go negotiate with Mr. Jiang."

Lu Yang: "..."

Is the human care in Seek Dao Sect too excessive?

"By the way, Eldest Senior Sister, we don’t believe that Qilin Immortal Senior was the one who assassinated Time Immortal Senior. His memories might have been altered by Yao Saint," said Lu Yang.

Alterations such as reality and memory became established facts once altered, without the need to maintain a Verbal Spell state constantly.

Yun Zhi nodded unsurprised, a look of expectation confirmed, "Just as I thought."

"You think so too?" Lu Yang was delighted, having spoken to gain support from Eldest Senior Sister.

"Of course, it’s just that..."

Yun Zhi stopped mid-sentence, realizing that too many people were around. Such things were not to be said openly, so she kept silent.

"But what?" Qilin Immortal eagerly wanted to know the reason.

Seeing Qilin Immortal’s urgency, Yun Zhi hesitated for a moment before saying, "Because you look rather weak."

"I..."

Qilin Immortal was choked off, turning to glare at three brothers barely holding back their laughter behind him.

"There’s another matter; the esteemed predecessors wish to unlock the World Seal to open Box World. What do you think about that?"

"Opening Box World? That’s a good idea," Yun Zhi revealed a faint smile.

Having lived in a Secret Realm since childhood, she had never seen the true stars. After Daoist Buyu took her out of the Secret Realm, although the sky was filled with dazzling stars, it was merely a shadow of the stars that once existed. She had then used the Golden Core in place of the stars.

Now that Box World was opening, she could fulfill her wish to witness the real starry sky.

"However, opening Box World involves many aspects and should not be done rashly," said Yun Zhi after smiling.

"That’s natural," Lu Yang knew his Eldest Senior Sister’s concerns mirrored his own. On the way here, he had already figured out how to proceed with the first step, "It would be best to call in the decision-makers from all major powers to sit down and come up with a standard together."

Among these major powers were Great Xia’s Jiang Ping’an, Demon Territory’s Jiang Lianyi, East Sea’s Ao Ling, Buddha Country’s Time Immortal. The Extreme Northern Lands lacked a unified power, so they would not be considered.

"Just right, I’m heading to Imperial City, I’ll talk to Mr. Jiang about this matter."

"So I’m responsible for notifying the rest?" Lu Yang took the initiative to volunteer.

"That won’t be necessary." Yun Zhi left these words, leaped into the air, transformed into a golden light and disappeared, leaving the crowd baffled.

What does ’That won’t be necessary’ mean? Who will notify the remaining Jiang Lianyi and Ao Ling?

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched slightly, he was the first to realize what Eldest Senior Sister meant and prepared to slip away before the situation became chaotic.

Unfortunately, it was already too late; the echoing sound of dragon and phoenix cries arose from the back mountain of Sky Gate Mountain.

"You dare come back!"

A dragon and a phoenix soared in the sky, their pupils burning with raging flames.

No wonder the rest didn’t need to be notified; Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi were already at the Seek Dao Sect.

Qilin Immortal’s complexion changed drastically upon seeing this, pulling over the Yingtian Immortal and Jiuchong Immortal to shield him.

"Qilin, handle family matters on your own," Yingtian Immortal and Jiuchong Immortal dodged at the crucial moment.

Then the generous Time Immortal shouted, "Both of you junior siblings, go ahead without worry; if things break, I can restore them using the Time Dao Fruit!"

The Yingtian Three Immortals tactfully moved away from the area to avoid any accidental injuries.

The combined attack of the dragon and phoenix was formidable, unparalleled as they swooped down from the sky, the figures of the dragon and phoenix enlarging in Qilin Immortal’s pupils.

Boom!!

The smoke billowed, and two graceful figures emerged from the dust, leaving only Qilin Immortal sprawled on the ground.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi snorted coldly, each grabbing one of Lu Yang’s arms.

"Elder Brother Lu Yang, didn’t we agree to deal with my husband together when he appears? Why didn’t you act?"

Lu Yang’s forehead was drenched in cold sweat. On the ground, Qilin Immortal was lifting his head, staring at Lu Yang with a terrifying gaze.

Even when Qilin Immortal knew that Lu Yang was proficient with the shameful past of Ancient Times, he had never looked at Lu Yang with such a gaze!

"Both of you senior sisters, I mean, both of you seniors, there must be some misunderstanding between us," Lu Yang murmured, sandwiched between Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, secretly lamenting his fate.

God knows, whenever I encounter such situations, I avoid them if I can; last time when Ao Ling proposed that they jointly teach Qilin Immortal a lesson, I teleported to the Extreme Northern Lands using Heaven and Earth in an Inch to suffer there.

Little Qiongqi and Jin Caiwei appeared behind, struggling to pull up Qilin Immortal from the ground, her height insufficient for the task.

She expressed her feelings at that moment, "Ah Shi, I knew you would come. I always believed in you!"

Feeling the gaze of everyone present, especially the cold, merciless eyes of Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi that seemed ready to kill, Qilin Immortal felt a desire to die.

"Caiwei, come here, don’t stand on his side," Ao Ling said coldly. They had searched the entire world for Qilin Immortal to no avail, clearly indicating he was intentionally avoiding them; the good fortune of his sudden appearance was too good to even contemplate.

Jin Caiwei glanced at Qilin Immortal and then at Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, making the tough decision to let go of Qilin Immortal and run to Lu Yang’s side.

In an instant, Qilin Immortal was again left all alone.

Any expectation from Immortal Fairy, who appeared to enjoy watching the drama unfold, was futile. Lu Yang prayed to the heavens, wishing for someone to help him break the deadlock.

"Second-in-command, you’re back!"

Yun Mengmeng appeared, her face overflowing with a naïve and radiant smile, and she lunged towards Lu Yang.

Lu Yang wore a look of utter despondence.

This isn’t the kind of escape I wanted.

Chapter 1260: Chapter 1259 The Great Bean Dynasty Meeting

"Oh right, Chief Housekeeper said our Immortal Lineage must have rules, we can’t go on like this."

Yun Mengmeng belatedly remembered and got off Lu Yang, pulling him up as well.

"Little Yang, as a Senior Brother, you have to satisfy your Junior Sister’s ideas. I will help you teach Qilin Immortal a lesson."

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi looked on with anticipation; they had been waiting for these words.

Lu Yang certainly didn’t want things to get out of hand, "Hey, Immortal Fairy, we agreed to use words, not force, right?"

"Do you mean to scold him? I’m not good at that, it’s all up to you."

"We’re not good at that either."

"...That’s not what I meant!" Lu Yang exclaimed, sweating profusely.

"Second-in-command, you do the scolding, I can learn by observing." Yun Mengmeng earnestly said, knowing there was much she needed to learn from the Second-in-command.

"Sister Mengmeng, learn something good."

"Second-in-command, you are the good example."

Yingtian Immortal interjected with advice for the two good brothers, "I’m telling you, visit Seek Dao Sect more often, it’s always lively here, and the dramas that unfold every day are unique."

Immortal Jiuchong and Time Immortal nodded in agreement, thinking it was livelier than the Ancient Times, and they chose the right place by visiting Seek Dao Sect.

"Three elder brothers, it’s been some days since we last met." Qinghe finally came out from the back mountain and greeted the three associated with Yingtian Immortal.

She too was eager to see Immortal Fairy, but unlike Ao Ling and others, she couldn’t afford to appear rushed. As a servant of Immortal Fairy, her every action while outdoors represented Immortal Fairy, so she had to be calm and composed.

After a good while of chaotic noise, everyone finally settled down.

They claimed Sky Gate Mountain as their own, seated themselves on the ground, and began telling Ao Ling and the others about the events that had unfolded in Zhongshan County.

"Just the place where my kitchen is located, I can show off my cooking skills. What will you eat, star core-filled dumplings or chili-filled buns?" The ever-eager Immortal Fairy was resolutely stopped by everyone.

"We had mush back in Buddha Country; it was quite good, we’ll skip eating here."

"Really? I saw your faces while eating mush, and you didn’t seem to enjoy it."

"You must have seen wrong."

"I just baked some small cookies, anyone wants some?" Yun Mengmeng presented two freshly baked cookies, earning grateful glances from the Four Ancient Immortals.

"No need to fuss, Immortal Fairy, we’ll just have these."

Everyone enjoyed the cookies, praising Yun Mengmeng’s baking skills endlessly, making her giggle foolishly, delighted by the compliments from such distinguished figures.

"Back in the Ancient Times, when Yao Saint committed suicide, he tried to blame it on me. I was so annoyed when I heard it that, despite being injured, I used Miss Yun’s body to confront Yao Saint like this..."

The crowd formed a circle, with Immortal Fairy in the center, making gestures to describe the scene.

Upon initially learning that all this was Yao Saint’s doing, Qinghe, Ao Ling, and Jiang Lianyi were extremely angry. But seeing how Immortal Fairy mimicked the actions, and imagining the pitiful state of Yao Saint, they couldn’t help but burst into laughter.

"And then I got tired of fighting, so I just self-detonated, blowing that scoundrel up..."

Everyone was overjoyed, reveling in the stories.

Towards the end, Immortal Fairy mentioned their plans to open Box World, and as expected, Ao Ling and others expressed their full support.

"We’d better notify Zhu Tian about this, have him come over for a meeting," Jiang Lianyi said.

Although she was the true ruler of Demon Territory, she wasn’t adept at managing, so Zhu Tian handled the specific affairs. It wouldn’t do for her to just listen while everyone else discussed details and precautions during the meeting.

...

In the Demon City Imperial Palace of Demon Territory.

Zhu Tian lay leisurely on the Emperor’s Chair, flipping through a newspaper, with stunning maids standing on either side holding trays of exotic fruits and treasures, not purchasable even with Spirit Stones.

Zhu Tian was in a good mood. Ever since he had opened trade channels with Great Xia, there had been mutual benefits, and Demon Territory had developed rapidly. Previously, goods from Great Xia sold in Demon Territory were expensive; now, they were quite affordable, earning him praises from the Demon Race as a wise and enlightened ruler.

"Zhu Tian."

A voice startled Zhu Tian, causing him to roll off the Emperor’s Chair in alarm.

Of course, the newcomer was Jiang Lianyi. Zhu Tian asked the maid to leave and said with a sycophantic smile, "Sister Jiang, what brings you here in such grand fashion? If you needed something, couldn’t you have just sent someone to pass the message?"

"Recently, a significant event has happened in the Cultivation World, and all the major forces plan to hold a meeting. The two of us will represent the Demon Territory."

"A meeting?" Zhu Tian instinctively felt a bit nervous.

"Don’t be nervous; they are all people we know."

Hearing this, Zhu Tian finally relaxed. As long as they were people he knew, it was fine.

...

Seek Dao Sect, Sky Gate Mountain.

When Zhu Tian arrived at the Seek Dao Sect, Eldest Senior Sister had already invited Jiang Pingan to the Sect. The attendees were all present.

He saw the setup for the meeting and his lips trembled as if he was about to cry, these familiar faces were too familiar.

How could all the Four Ancient Immortals be here?!

And there were Immortal Fairy, Yun Zhi, Jiang Pingan... all Immortals.

He had just awakened and was very capable of biding his time, collecting information about the current world. He learned that no Semi-Immortal had appeared and thought he might be the only one, so he decided to claim the title of Emperor in the Demon Territory.

Now it seemed there were almost more Immortals than Semi-Immortals.

It was never like this even in the ancient golden age.

"Little Zhu, I heard you are called the Demon Emperor in the Demon Territory?" Qilin Immortal beckoned Zhu Tian over.

Zhu Tian approached with fear and terror, showing a smile uglier than crying. The person he feared most was Qilin Immortal. He had claimed the title of Demon Emperor under the name of Qilin Immortal, and during the founding ceremony, he even fought with Qilin Immortal’s wife.

Especially since Qilin Immortal was his Upper Dao Fruit; the other could control him with just a thought.

"It’s just the little demons calling that in fun; I’ll go back and shut them up right away!," Zhu Tian quickly expressed his loyalty.

"That’s up to you. I heard from Little Friend Lu that you manage the Demon Territory well. Keep up the good work," Qilin Immortal said, patting Zhu Tian’s shoulder with a smile.

Zhu Tian didn’t expect Qilin Immortal to say this, and was pleasantly surprised.

Following Brother Lu surely was the right choice; Brother Lu even spoke highly of him in front of Qilin Immortal.

Zhu Tian wanted to thank Lu Yang in person, but he noticed Lu Yang was talking with someone else and decided to wait.

"Sister Mengmeng, what are you doing?" Lu Yang asked. Yun Mengmeng was leaning over a table writing something.

"I’m making nameplates for the meeting."

"Nameplates?"

Lu Yang still didn’t understand.

"I’m the Minister of Rites, so this is my responsibility, of course I have to prepare these."

"What does it have to do with today’s meeting?"

Yun Mengmeng stood up and counted on her fingers, "You see, the Chief Housekeeper is the Emperor, the Second-in-command is you, a pillar nation minister."

"Little Lotus is the Historian, Little Ling Lianyi, Caiwei, the three sisters are Great Generals, and I’m the Minister of Rites."

"Xiao Zhi is the Minister of War, Senior Jiang Pingan is the Imperial College Sacrificial Officer, Emperor Xia is the Prime Minister, and Zhu Tian is the Minister of the Ministry of Industry."

"Isn’t this the Great Bean Dynasty holding a meeting?"

Once Yun Mengmeng explained this, Lu Yang finally realized that in today’s meeting, except for the Four Ancient Immortals, everyone was from the Great Bean Dynasty.

Truly worthy of the Great Bean Dynasty, everyone held high and powerful positions, with no idle members.

Not to mention idle members, there weren’t even any common folk.

Immortal Fairy also realized this and flew over to the Four Ancient Immortals to ask, "I’ve established a Great Bean Dynasty, do you want to join?"

"The Great Bean Dynasty?" Immortal Jiuchong was a bit confused, "What official positions will we have if we join?"

"Common folk."

Chapter 1261: Chapter 1260: Grand Assembly of Heaven’s Opening

According to historical records, at the dawn of the Great Bean Dynasty, even though there were ministers who wrought chaos within the imperial court, under the wise and martial Emperor Dou’s leadership, the nation flourished splendidly.

The common people could converse with Emperor Dou at will, and could even participate in the imperial council, expressing their opinions and suggestions, a practice unprecedented in all past dynasties.

After being persuaded by Fairy Eternity, the Four Ancient Immortals were fortunate to join the Great Bean Dynasty.

"Here, the Chief Housekeeper said this is for you." Yun Mengmeng gave each of the Four Ancient Immortals a blank card, signifying "plain identity," and stuck it to their chests.

"This is a little gift for you, welcome to our Great Bean Dynasty!" Yun Mengmeng also gave each of them a small paper bag.

"Thank you, Little Friend, you are kind."

As Yun Zhi’s close sister and the Third Boss of the Immortal Lineage, to call someone Little Friend was quite proper.

The Four Ancient Immortals were somewhat surprised, wondering if these preparations had been made in advance.

When they opened the bags, they found a pack of sunflower seeds and sweets.

Not only them, but everyone attending the meeting also received a pack, cracking seeds and chatting away.

After Yun Mengmeng left, Zhu Tian finally found the opportunity to express his sincerity to Lu Yang. His words deeply moved Lu Yang, "Brother Lu, if you ever need anything that Little Zhu can help with, just say the word. If you even want the stars in the sky, I will pluck them for you!"

"You can pluck stars?" Lu Yang looked at him oddly, thinking to himself that this is truly a Demon Emperor’s grand claim.

Zhu Tian, hearing the skepticism in Lu Yang’s voice, couldn’t have that, "Of course, I’m not bragging. We ancient cultivators find picking stars and capturing moons a very common post-dinner entertainment."

"Don’t believe me, Brother Lu? Just wait until the meeting is over and I’ll pick one for you!"

"No, no, no, I’m not interested in plucking stars," Lu Yang quickly grabbed Zhu Tian, thinking that even the Tiger Clan isn’t as bold as you are, and it would be quite the event if Zhu Tian really went and plucked a star.

"If Nation Master Zhu has the time, perhaps craft a set of wooden tea utensils."

"Tea utensils?" Zhu Tian’s mind flashed through various types of tea utensils and he readily agreed, "No problem."

He decided he would begin crafting them after returning.

"Well then, I won’t bother you any longer, Brother Lu. Call on me if there’s anything you need." Zhu Tian waved goodbye enthusiastically. He and Lu Yang weren’t that close, so it was good to improve relations with a brief contact, but hanging around for too long might have the opposite effect.

Zhu Tian quickly set his sights on the next target of the meeting.

"Emperor Jiang, long time no see," Zhu Tian approached Emperor Xia.

Zhu Tian actually had no particular business with Emperor Xia, he just knew that among those at the meeting, when it came to status and cultivation level, if Emperor Xia dared to claim he was the lowest, Zhu Tian dared to claim the second lowest. The unspoken rule since ancient times is that those at the bottom must band together for warmth.

"Your Majesty, everyone has arrived. Whom do you think we should send to organize the meeting?" Yun Zhi came over and asked. Originally, she planned to organize the meeting, but then she thought that since she was now a person of the Great Bean Dynasty, it was only proper to ask Fairy Eternity to make the decision.

"Of course, it should be Little Yang," Fairy Eternity replied without hesitation.

"Ah? Me?"

Lu Yang had not expected that such a significant responsibility would fall on him. He was just in the Early Tribulation Stage. Except for Emperor Xia who had a lower cultivation level than him, his participation in this meeting was purely because of his connections.

"You’re my pillar of the nation, aren’t you? As the highest-ranking official, it’s certainly you."

"Indeed, I also agree that it should be Junior Brother who presides over the meeting."

"The Emperor chooses the capable and promotes the virtuous, truly an act of a wise ruler," Yun Zhi echoed.

"Of course, who else could I be?"

Lu Yang: "..."

Was this what resided within Junior Brother Li’s body?

"That means you can master the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype now." Immortal Fairy was surprised, Little Yang mastered it quickly.

Lu Yang analyzed, realizing that such quick mastery couldn’t be solely attributed to intuition: "Perhaps it’s related to my experiences outside the Box World. Having died once outside it, I had essentially undergone a reincarnation, which, by coincidence, matched the intent of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype."

"Do you want to become a Semi-Immortal of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype?"

Lu Yang shook his head. Possessing the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype merely meant reincarnation after death, not the effect he desired.

Yet he had a hunch, feeling that the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype was somehow linked to his becoming a Semi-Immortal.

As soon as there was a stir at the door of the abode, Yun Mengmeng swayed the hammock, spinning in mid-air before landing in front of Lu Yang.

"Second-in-command, have you finished your seclusion?"

Lu Yang shook his head, "No, I came out for a break because I got tired along the way."

"Of course."

The two descended the mountain and Lu Yang found, to his puzzlement, that the sect was unusually deserted compared to normal days.

Yun Mengmeng pointed towards the entrance of the Seek Dao Sect, "Today is the day we recruit new disciples. Everyone has gone there to maintain order."

"So it’s already the second day of the second month again," Lu Yang said, somewhat in a daze. He thought back to when he was very naive, riding on Old Meng’s carriage, even discussing how to cheat in front of Eldest Senior Sister. So many years had passed since then.

When they arrived at the entrance of the sect, the first test of root bone was still the same, with Elder Brother Dai still sitting at the front conducting the tests.

The only difference from the time Lu Yang participated was an astonishing surge in the number of young men and women applying to the Seek Dao Sect—more than double the previous amount.

"Look, is that Lu Yang?"

A young boy in line excitedly pointed at Lu Yang.

The reason so many people came to the Seek Dao Sect was precisely because of the reputations of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

These two geniuses shone brightly, young in age but with experiences far richer than those of many older cultivators who had passed their Tribulation.

"Right there at the bamboo forest entrance, look."
