"I don’t know."

The previously well-ordered line of young men and women became slightly restless; Lu Yang suddenly the center of attention, forcing Elder Brother Dai to step in to maintain order and not forgetting to glare back at Lu Yang in the process.

Although Lu Yang hadn’t done anything wrong, he still retreated guiltily back into the bamboo forest out of sight from the young men and women after being glared at by Dai Bufan.

"Senior Brother."

"Senior Brother Lu."

"Junior Sister Tao, Junior Brother Li, you are here to help organize the initiation test?" Lu Yang said with a smile, his hands clasped in greeting.

"Yes, Elder Brother Dai said there was a shortage of reliable help, so he called us over," Li Haoran said with a smile.

"Senior Brother Lu, we haven’t seen each other for a long time," Tao Yaoye said with a hint of complaint in her voice, especially seeing Yun Mengmeng so close to Lu Yang.

"I’ve been quite busy recently, really didn’t have time," Lu Yang said, feeling somewhat embarrassed.

While chatting idly, Lu Yang’s gaze occasionally drifted over to the young men and women to see how their testing was progressing.

Tao Yaoye noticed Lu Yang’s gaze and remarked, "It’s easy to be reminded of when we took the test ourselves, isn’t it?"

"Yes," Li Haoran agreed with the same nostalgia.

They had all been obscure figures once upon a time. In the blink of an eye, so many years had passed, and now they had become figures spoken of by everyone.

At these words, Lu Yang was stunned; he had an epiphany, realizing his understanding of reincarnation had been too narrow. With Li Haoran as an example, he thought that only the transmigration of souls counted as reincarnation.

What’s to say that the recurrence of similar events isn’t a kind of reincarnation?

Chapter 1266: Chapter 1265: Lu Yang’s Dao Fruit Outline

Lu Yang carefully recalled the events he had experienced, each time he left the Sect over some trifling matter to gain experience in the outside world, only for the situation to escalate to an uncontrollable extent, which was in fact, a cycle of reincarnation. frёewebnoѵēl.com

Lu Yang murmured softly under his breath, a hint of brightness in his eyes, as he finally understood the nature of the Dao Fruit that could help his Eldest Senior Sister.

He was uncertain which Dao Fruit embryos or Dao Fruits could bring him the knowledge he needed, so he had to resort to the most straightforward approach, to keep trying.

Some knowledge was easily understood by Lu Yang, resulting in a short stay; some were entirely new to him and difficult to comprehend, hence the prolonged stays.

And the place he stayed the longest was the Great Xia Imperial City.

There were two of the founders of Great Xia, Jiang Pingan and Meng Junzi, as well as the Four Ancient Immortals who had been invited to discuss the Dao – a total of six Immortals.

If it were not for the dark hand behind the scenes, this would be one of the reasons why Lu Yang supported the unsealing.

Lu Yang began an immeasurable period of seclusion in his Abode.

The Time Path was the main body of the "bridge," and the other gains along the way were also parts of this "bridge."

Chapter 1268: Chapter 1267: Strange Trace Origin Dao Fruit Outline

For instance, a Peak Tribulation Stage cultivator deploying the Great Divine Skill "Five Thunders Technique" would definitely be inferior to to the Thunder Skill deployed by a Tribulation Dao Fruit Prototype.

Chapter 1269: Chapter 1268: The Magic Skill I’ve Learned is the Correct One!

"The result of ’Trace Origin’ itself?"

"Even though the ancient ancestors lived in harsh conditions, battling against heaven and earth, since they had created True Fire magic skills, it meant they had the very basic ability to defend themselves, so hunting wild beasts wasn’t difficult."

"Once they had taken care of food and warmth, the next natural step was to figure out how to eat better."

"Seasonings like chili, cumin, and sugar must have been hard to find during Ancient Times, so the ancient ancestors created ’Three Flavored True Fire,’ a fire that could enhance flavors—capable of both cooking the meat and making it tastier, killing two birds with one stone!"

"And there’s another thing, the existence of writing had just begun in Ancient Times. Could our ancestors have come up with a sophisticated name like ’Samadhi’ for True Fire? Definitely not."

"They interpreted the words literally; the True Fire had three flavors, so they named it ’Three Flavored True Fire.’"

"Then for some reason, Three Flavored True Fire was lost, or only the name survived, and later generations changed it wildly, turning it into Samadhi True Fire."

"Look, does that sound logical?"

Clapping came from both sides simultaneously, Fairy Eternity and Yun Mengmeng applauding and vocalizing support for Lu Yang.

"Little Yang’s ideas are just what this Immortal wanted to express."

"The Second-in-command makes such reasonable points."

Meng Jingzhou, "..."

Don’t think that just because your Immortal Lineage has many people you are correct.

"Then how do you explain the Golden Bird True Flame?"

Before Lu Yang could answer, Yun Mengmeng raised her hand and answered first, "I know this one, definitely the ancient Gold Crow lineage had two legs, and later they mutated to have three."

The biggest difference between Golden Bird True Flame and Gold Crow True Flame is the loss of one leg.

Lu Yang echoed, "See, that’s the answer."

The three from the Immortal Lineage agreed, leaving Meng Jingzhou with some doubts, "... Maybe you should test another magic skill?"

Old Lu didn’t just learn the two True Fire skills crookedly.

"Let me try Earth Shrinking and Shrink Inch."

Lu Yang stood up without hesitation and, as usual, employed Earth Shrinking.

With a whoosh, he burrowed underground. Meng Jingzhou wanted to observe Old Lu’s underground movements using his Spiritual Sense, but Lu Yang moved through the soil so quickly it was surprising, and he soon exceeded the range of Meng Jingzhou’s Spiritual Sense.

When Lu Yang emerged from the ground, he was holding a handful of black soil.

Meng Jingzhou’s pupils dilated, "Is this the black soil in contact with the World Seal at the very bottom?!"

"Indeed."

This meant Lu Yang had just dived from the surface straight to the deepest part of the ground in one breath!

"After I performed Earth Shrinking, I still uncontrollably activated the Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype. Compared to usual, my burrowing speed this time was very fast, so fast that not even the king of earthworms, the Silver Ring King Worm, could catch up with me!"

Lu Yang was quite proud; it meant he was unmatched in the art of burrowing!

"Shrink Inch."

Lu Yang used Shrink Inch and turned into a tiny figure an inch tall.

Yun Mengmeng, seeing such a tiny Lu Yang for the first time, found it very amusing and poked him.

Lu Yang felt that this image compromised the dignity of the Second-in-command, so he gradually expanded from one inch to three inches, then to one zhang and three zhangs... eventually becoming a giant a thousand zhang tall!

However, his growing process was like that of bamboo, growing section by section, increasing only inch by inch.

"Ha ha, now I can perform the true Law of Heaven and Earth!" Lu Yang laughed loudly, his voice resonant and loud enough to shatter the clouds in the sky.

Soon after, Lu Yang returned to his original size.

"How do you explain ’Shrinking Ground Into Inches?’" Meng Jingzhou was a bit convinced by Lu Yang’s previous nonsensical explanations,

mainly because he couldn’t think of any other explanation.

Neither Fairy Eternity nor Yun Mengmeng answered; at a critical moment, Lu Yang reliably provided an explanation.

"It’s easy to explain. Just now I grew in increments of ’inches,’ which suggests that ’Shrink Inch’ might have been used for standardized measurements during Ancient Times. ’Earth Shrinking’? Literally, it means shrinking into the earth."

Meng Jingzhou still didn’t understand, "How did two unrelated words end up being put together?"

"’Even if I have to dig three feet into the ground, I will find him.’ Does that sound familiar?"

Meng Jingzhou nodded; who hasn’t heard this saying?

"Fairy, have you heard this saying during Ancient Times?"

"I have."

Lu Yang stroked his chin, speculating, "According to my guess, this saying existed in Ancient Times."

"For example, if something was stolen from the tribe, the Clan Leader would order the entire clan to find it, even if it meant digging three feet into the ground."

"But how much is three feet? It’s hard to say, so our ancestors would become thirty inches tall, which is three feet tall, then shrink into the ground. Now, wouldn’t that show exactly how much three feet deep is?"

Meng Jingzhou, "..."

Old Lu, I wanted to believe you, but could your explanation be a bit more plausible?

"Don’t believe me? Ask Junior Brother Man Gu. When he first saw the term ’Shrinking Ground Into Inches,’ did he think it was a Space Spell?"

Then, Lu Yang performed ’Heaven and Earth in an Inch,’ disappearing from his spot.

When Lu Yang returned, he held sand from Buddha Country, snow from the Extreme Northern Lands, seawater from East Sea... proving how many places he had visited in just a short time.

Before, when Lu Yang used ’Heaven and Earth in an Inch,’ he would be randomly transported to a cliffside, but after activating the Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype, the result was quite different—he could finally choose which cliffside to appear on.

"So what does this prove? This proves the magic skills I learned are the correct ones, and all of you have been learning them wrong," Lu Yang crossed his arms, looking as smug as could be, having waited so long for this day of vindication after being slandered for so long.

I knew my magic talent was so good; how could I possibly learn incorrectly?

After such a lengthy spiel, Meng Jingzhou suspected that the last sentence was really what Old Lu wanted to say.

Chapter 1270: Chapter 1269: Bipedal Golden Crow

Chapter 1271: Chapter 1270: Difficult to Explain Predictions of the Future

Was there a relationship between these three?

Chapter 1272: Chapter 1271: Unsealing the Seal

A pair of eyes, shadowy and deep, fixed upon Lu Yang, yet no one perceived his presence; it was as if he existed not in this world, untouched by the myriad causality.

The world was silent, all eyes on the Four Ancient Immortals; it was as if they were the only four in heaven and earth.

Lu Yang watched eagerly as Immortal Jiuchong used his ability to dim the brightness of the Sun a little.

Should such an event be reported as it is?

Chapter 1273: Chapter 1272: The Emergence of Anomalies

At this moment in the Cultivation World, whether mortals or cultivators, no matter which continent’s creatures, all put down what they were doing, craning their necks eagerly to watch the Four Ancient Immortals, transforming into a four-colored stream of light, fleeing far away, out of sight.

Even the most keen-sighted cultivators cannot stand on one continent and see another.

"Are the Four Ancient Immortals going to break the seal?"

"It should be, right?"

Although there were speculations when the Four Ancient Immortals appeared, after all, it was just a guess; who would dare to conclude without witnessing it themselves?

Just as everyone was in doubt, a series of dull thunderclaps sounded overhead, and dark clouds obscured the sky.

"Why is there sudden thunder?"

"At such a critical moment, why is there thunder? Who will disperse it?" A Unification Cultivator frowned, even if he couldn’t see what the Four Ancient Immortals were doing, nothing should obstruct the view. He wanted to cast a spell to fan away the dark clouds and thunder.

"No, this is not ordinary thunder!" A sensitive cultivator stopped his companion, "Look closely, there are changes in this thunder!"

Silver thunder pierced through the dark clouds, rolling in the sky, and the thickness of the thunder was surprisingly consistent, like lines, forming various images.

"The images are of the Four Ancient Immortals!"

Against the backdrop of the dark clouds, using thunder as paint, silver snakes danced, outlining the scene of the Four Ancient Immortals joining hands to open the heavens!

At this moment, if someone stood at the position of the Sun, they would see that the skies above all five continents were covered by thick leaden clouds, impenetrable to light.

This meant that all creatures were fortunate to witness the process of the heavens opening!

Mortals and low to mid-level cultivators were just glad to be able to continue watching the opening process, but the hearts of the Great Cultivators were filled with shock and awe; from ancient times to the present, no one had heard of such variations in thunder and lightning!

"Could it be because this moment holds an extraordinary significance in history, having an unusual implication for the heaven and earth, thus Heaven wants to record this moment with thunder and lightning?"

"Yes, it must be so!"

...

"If I and the Emperor had not lived in the Fairy Palace and had stayed in Great Qian, it would never have perished!"

Guan Shanhai snorted at such claims: "The downfall of Great Qian is the inevitability of history, it has nothing to do with whether you lived in the Fairy Palace or not. The number of Divine Positions is fixed, and each of you Divine Monarchs occupies one. It’s impossible that you would have willingly ceded them to others."

"This led to those below lacking space to rise. The entire dynasty was stagnant. Your Divine Monarchs were merely occupying their positions without fulfillment, and the cultivators below would inevitably rebel. There would always be cultivators who secretly became Semi-Immortals, Immortals, and overthrew Great Qian."

"By comparison, our Great Yu abandoned the Divine Position system from the beginning and established the Imperial Teacher system. If it wasn’t for Wu Yao’s obstruction and I was still in Great Yu, the successive Imperial Teachers would definitely remain loyal to assist the emperors, and Great Yu would never have been doomed."

The Mid-heaven Emperor Lord snorted coldly, with utmost disdain: "It’s just your wishful thinking; your Great Yu is filled with influential families. With each passing emperor, countless families rise, contending with previous families for resources. Family strife, internal chaos within the state, how could the Imperial Teacher system resolve that?"

"If you ask me, The Controller said it best, had I and The Controller stayed in Great Qian, resolved the issue of Divine Monarchs, Great Qian would surely have been passed down through a thousand generations..."

"Even before the founding, Wu Yao and I had researched it; your problem with Divine Monarchs is unsolvable, fundamentally flawed..."

Leaders of both factions argued endlessly about why their own powers had fallen into decay and perished, with neither side yielding to the other.

The Semi-Immortals and those at the Transcendence Tribulation Stage from both sides dared not speak as they were essentially the "Divine Monarchs" and "Family Ancestors."

"Look, there are changes in the sky!"

Someone shouted, drawing the attention of all the prisoners.

The prisoners saw the densely packed dark clouds above their heads, and the thunder outlining the Sky Opening Map, causing the leaders of both sides to temporarily cease their conflict.

"Is the sky opening?"

"What a clever move, using the Tribulation Dao Fruit to induce a Heavenly Tribulation; I’m afraid it’s not just us who can see it above our heads, the entire Cultivation World can witness this scene."

Mid-heaven Emperor Lord clicked his tongue in admiration: "I thought our Great Qian’s Sealing God Ceremony was already extravagant enough, truly worthy of the Four Ancient Immortals, their gestures are even grander."

The Controller slapped his thigh, filled with regret: "Why didn’t I think to use the Dao Fruit like this? If I had used the Enlightenment Tao Fruit to enlighten the Sealing God Platform, I could have pretended to be the will of Heaven sealing gods!"

At this moment, Guan Shanhai and the Controller shared the same thought, equally regretful: "Our Great Yu’s founding ceremony was too conservative, originally I should have used the Imprinting Dao Fruit to imprint a bunch of top-grade Spirit Stones and set them off like fireworks!"

...

Demon Territory.

Qinghe, clutching a Treasure Bag, feels like she has found an incredible treasure; these seeds inside are already extinct now. If planted at Sky Gate Mountain, the adults would surely reward her.

"Why has it turned dark?"

Qinghe looked up, the skies were covered with dark clouds, as four majestic figures were evidently unsealing the seals.

Thud.

Qinghe stared blankly at the sky, the Treasure Bag falling to the ground.

In this moment, the unsealing by the four brothers meant that the adults had left seclusion and gone to Imperial City. Not just the adults, but everyone she knew should be present there.

And she missed the adults coming out of seclusion?!

...

Above the skies of the Wuling Continent, the Four Ancient Immortals perform the Law of Heaven and Earth, transforming into Sky Opening Giants.

Beneath the feet of these four giants, golden lotuses appeared; Earth Bursting Golden Lotuses blooming with each step they took.

Millions of Demon Beast illusions appeared, among them were such extinct species of Demon Beasts. These beasts bowed down to the Qilin Immortal in unison, a grand gathering of all demons.

The Yin Yang Qi merged, branding the Tai Chi Diagram onto the entire land of Wuling, with Two Elements Create Four Symbols, Four Symbols Birth Eight Diagrams, endless and boundless.

Moreover, the yellow Du bell tolls, declaring to all under heaven, with the temporal flow faintly visible, and the Nian Beast galloping and leaping upon these flows...

All these extraordinary phenomena appeared simultaneously around the world, astounding all who saw them.

Such phenomena had never occurred before, yet today they emerged all at once, and anyone who witnessed this scene would feel that the unsealing of the Four Ancient Immortals and the opening of heaven and earth was a great feat, one that even Heaven commemorates with extraordinary signs.

Numerous cultivators were sparked with the aspiration of ’a man should strive to be like this’, resolving to practice cultivation rigorously, aspiring to follow in the footsteps of the Four Ancient Immortals.

Lu Yang and the others were observing from not too far away, trying their best to avoid the Recording Orbs.

Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, Jin Caiwei were each holding Recording Orbs, capturing this scene from different angles.

"Don’t you want to show your face in front of the Recording Orb, Fairy?" Lu Yang asked.

Fairy Eternity floated beside Lu Yang, without phenomena, without momentum, without Divine Ability, like an ordinary Soul.

"No, showing off is such a hassle."

Compared to the Four Immortals, Fairy Eternity is low-key. This can be deduced from the Four Ancient Immortals often holding sermons to discuss how to maintain an Immortal’s demeanor, while Fairy Eternity merely listens on the side.

If it was just to unseal, there was no need for so many complex processes and methods; just like Fairy Eternity who quietly spurred on beside, others wouldn’t even notice her activating the Dao Fruit.

But clearly, the Four Ancient Immortals had their own ideas.

Chapter 1274: Chapter 1273: Opening the Heavens

The sound of the Great Dao is echoing, reverberating between heaven and earth, with countless ancient runes appearing around the Four Ancient Immortals, these runes being the vessels for their Dao Fruits.

The ancient runes flicker and merge into the Wuling Continent, touching the seal at its base.

The World Seal was jointly created by the Four Ancient Immortals utilizing their respective Dao Fruits.

The Yin-Yang Dao Fruit uses the Yin Yang Qi as the foundation for the barrier.

The Time Dao Fruit allows time to reverse, repairing the barrier should it shatter.

The Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit makes the barrier emerge unscathed from the same attack.

The Tribulation Dao Fruit has attached the "Infinite Tribulation" to the barrier, an endless and irregular challenge that can only be violently broken.

The interwoven abilities of the four Dao Fruits mean that even if the four of them attacked at once, the seal could not be undone.

Only by them mobilizing the Dao Fruits to weaken the barrier, and then with the help of Fairy Eternity’s infinite self-detonation, could the seal be broken.

"Not enough, we’re just short of a bit!" Immortal Jiuchong said in a deep voice.

"But this is all the strength we have!" Kirin Immortal said, reluctantly accepting that despite their all-out effort, this was as far as they could go.

Just a little bit more, just that tiny bit!

Time Immortal remained silent, only persistently animating the runes to decipher the seal.

Their voices were not loud, yet they held a sacredness and the weight of history, reaching the entire Cultivation World through the Heavenly Tribulation.

The entire Cultivation World felt the disappointment of the Four Ancient Immortals.

Yingtian Immortal slowly closed his eyes, as if having made a certain decision: "No, this is not all our strength, there’s one last method left!"

The other three Immortals were simultaneously shocked: "You mean to strike the seal horizontally with our Immortal Bodies?!"

Yingtian Immortal nodded: "Yes, only this method is left!"

"But that way, we would..."

"There are no ’buts’!"

The Four Ancient Immortals finally reached a unanimous decision, each flying to the four corners of Wuling Continent, suddenly self-detonating, wrenching at the hearts of all.

After the self-detonation, the Four Ancient Immortals were drenched in Immortal Blood, an especially tragic sight.

"Still not enough, continue!" They gritted their teeth and continued to self-detonate.

The world was moved, speechless at this scene, the Four Ancient Immortals sacrificing far too much to unseal the seal.

Some people couldn’t help but shed tears at the sight.

The sound of the Great Dao that spread throughout the Cultivation World now carried a particularly desolate tone.

Lu Yang was also moved, the performance of the Four Ancient Immortals was truly masterful.

To unseal the seal, one needed to self-detonate as an Immortal on top of weakening the seal.

Thus, the four Yingtian Immortals requested Fairy Eternity to temporarily bestow upon them the "Immortal status," their feigned collision with the seal and resulting explosion masking the reality of their continuous self-detonation.

Don’t be fooled by their blood-drenched forms; in fact, they were not hurt at all.

The only thing real here was their Immortal Blood, which Lu Yang heard was drawn from their own bodies when they first initiated the plan.

However, there was one minor issue, Lu Yang wanted to ask, why would Yingtian Immortal and Time Immortal bleed?

One with an Immortal Golden Body, the other with a Faith Golden Body, do they even have a drop of blood?

Yun Zhi explained on the side: "Their Immortal Blood was borrowed from Immortal Jiuchong and Kirin Immortal."

Lu Yang: "..."

Truly the bond between brothers, that even such a thing would be lent.

Boom——

With the last self-detonation, the Four Ancient Immortals, exhausted, were covered in wounds and had no strength even to fly, collapsing powerlessly to the ground.

But the attention of the world was not on the Four Ancient Immortals.

For the seal of the Land of No Spirit had been broken.

Crack——Crack——

The plates of the Land of No Spirit fractured, continually collapsing, gradually separating from the surrounding four continents and no longer in contact.

...

"Father, it’s late at night, time to sleep." The young man carried a cup of tea onto the high platform, his father being the Director of the Imperial Astronomical Observatory.

This is the location of the Imperial Astronomical Observatory of the White Horse Dynasty, the highest building of the White Horse Dynasty, built to facilitate the observation of celestial patterns, calculate the solar terms, and establish the calendar.

The Director yawned, "Is it already that time?"

"Father, you often say that the movement of the stars follows a pattern, and our Imperial Astronomical Observatory has a history of a thousand years, having long summarized the laws of star movement. Why deprive yourself of sleep to observe the celestial patterns?" The young man complained somewhat, as he couldn’t sleep comfortably with his father awake.

"When I was young, I used to observe celestial patterns around this time; it has become a habit," the Director said, as an older father, he cherished his son immensely.

"But you’re also right, our Imperial Astronomical Observatory has already grasped the laws of star movement, there’s no need to work so hard."

"Especially this Mysterious Land above our heads, unchanged through the ages, more observation is useless."

The Director smiled and pointed at the endless sky that was filled with mysterious legends, the Divine World.

Since the birth of civilization on this planet, that world has been floating above, with many stars in front of that continent, as insignificant as dust.

To maintain orthodoxy through the dynasties, they all professed belief in the Divine Continent.

According to their legends, enlightened ones could ascend to the Immortal World during daylight, which is the Divine World.

"Although the position of the Director will sooner or later be yours, after all, within the entire White Horse Dynasty, only we grasp the laws of the stars. But you must not be too negligent, I teach you the laws of the stars to be firmly remembered; this is the foundation of our standing."

"For example, in recent years the sea level rose, flooding the coastal towns, His Majesty asked us, the Imperial Astronomical Observatory, for the reason, we say it’s because His Majesty’s accession was illegitimate, causing the anger of heaven and resentment among the people. Guess if His Majesty believes what we say?"

The Director once again looked up to the sky, looking at that endless world with a sneer on his lips, "As for this Divine World, it’s nothing but an unfounded legend."

"There are no immortals in this world, the immortals in the legends are just the ignorance of the ancients, mistaking martial artists for immortals, perpetuating the error."

It wasn’t unusual for martial artists, capable of lifting a thousand catties of stone, to be mistaken for immortals.

The Director stretched his neck, ready to sleep, when he noticed his son looking up into the sky, dumbfounded.

The Director felt somewhat relieved; his son was ignorant and had learned the laws and their implications regarding the stars only superficially, and he was worried about his future.

Now that his son was interested in the celestial patterns, it could be considered a return to the right path.

The Director patted his son’s shoulder with relief, "All right, stop looking, go to sleep. If you really want to watch, sleep well during the day, and then you can watch all you want at night."

The son did not reply; his body was puppet-like, pointing stiffly into the sky.

The Director looked up and was so frightened that he sat down abruptly on the ground, clutching his heart, his teeth chattering.

That unchanging Divine World was trembling and breaking apart, followed by blinding light emanating from the fissures.

Merely the light that shone from the cracks turned the night of their White Horse Dynasty into day, reversing Yin and Yang, upending the world.

Centuries of heritage, experiences passed down by the Imperial Astronomical Observatory through generations, vanished to nothing at that moment.

The Director’s mind went blank, not even aware of what he was saying, as if talking in his sleep.

"The Divine World... has opened..."
